，並關於婦女及家庭問題的著作，供應給本社，還有劉王立明女士自已的一本文藝創作「生命的波濤」亦將出版問世；以上各位女士的精心偉構，久已風行海內，殊用不着我來介紹。工藝部主任是張學海女士，這一部的物品包括刺繡製造等各手工出品，除女子家事高級職業學校，及婦孺教育院担任一部份外，其餘已向北平紹興等各方面分頭接洽。食品部主任則由吳淑卿女土担任，關於這一部的出品，以中西茶點為重心，那可完全是　　家事學校的成績。其餘還有幾位職員，共同襄理。不過我們都是以服務社會為天職，所以是沒有薪水的，除非本社有盈餘，除去開支及辦慈善事業之外，大家纔得平均分配，不過現在還須添聘能操流利英語，稍諳簿記的女職員一位，如有這樣人才而又有興趣服務社會的，可以詳述自己的所長，寫信到我這裏—華龍路元昌里十四號—來接洽。至於今後的方針，實在也沒有什麼可以奉吿，不過在目前我們女子或多或少的總是處在雙層或甚至三層壓迫下面，這是無席諱言的，關於女子的一切事業現在還完全在萌芽時代，擁護的固然多，存心摧殘的也决不會少，深願羣策羣力，能夠由上海為出發點，慢慢的推行到全國去。我們明知在現在經濟恐慌時代，一切事業都不容易辦得好，但你若不能與惡劣環境相搏戰，去克復一切困難，那你便更沒有生路了。」　　「女士交際廣闊，担任經理一職當然勝任愉快，女土的履歷和私生活也肯宣布一些嗎？」　　「我這次謬膺這個重任，實在慚愧得很，雖則經婦女節制恊會中西各董事議决委我担任，然而我總覺得通去學校生活過得太久，自己委實還是　學生而不是個商人，雖然自從離開北大以後，在政界服務了一年多，後來又在教育界和商界奔走了七八年，但根據過去的經騐，作一番自我的批評，恐怕不能勝任，幸得各界友朋的鼓勵和贊助，又有這許多同志的帮忙，單就這裹張吳二位女士的精明幹練來說，已足為我的好幫手了，所以就勉效棉薄，不然或許難免限越呢。至於私生活，實在太簡單，除了每天晚上往量才補習學校讀一點日文外，沒有什麼可以報吿，並且前天女子月刋社已派人來訪問我過，為避免重複起見，不再說罷。說到交際廣闊，那可根本不敢當，我自從踏上社會纔小到十年，所認識的軍警政商學各界人士也不過幾千人，至於在社會上比較有地位的則僅幾百人而已，那裹夠得上交際兩個字。」　　「聽說女士也是唐冠玉女士　所發起的　國女子書　會的會員，將來貴社開幕的時候，大作想亦不少吧？」　　「見笑得很，雖然有。幅署欵胡　馨的就是拙作，但　向沒有時間去練習，僅僅是暇時的一種消遺，記得三年前承謝无量，陳立廷，徐悲鴻，章士釗等諸位先生為我訂了一個潤例，可是與各界酬應的大小書件至今恐還小滿百幅，眞是生疏得很，將來還希海　各大方家多多指教。」時事硏究貌合神離的英法關係  召琪　　英法兩國都是國際聯盟的主要支持者，倫敦和巴黎的外交家向來都是挾日內瓦以自利的，在這點上可說它們並沒有衝突。但戰後的英國外交，主要的是在努力維持歐洲之均勢，以保存不　顚帝國在歐洲的固有的地位，並維持它在非洲和亞洲的殖民地的權利；而去蘭西的外交視綫則是集中在萊茵河對岸，集中在柏林的；因此，英法兩國的外交政策雖同以國聯為基點，但它們各自的目標卻根本不相同，以致使倫敦與巴黎的意志在根本上就不易結合。　　最近因為莫索里尼遠征來非，企圖獨吞阿比西尼亞，使英人感到非洲殖民地受着威脅，地中海上原有的勢力為之動　，所以，當意阿開火的消息傳出後，英國馬上就在日內瓦大聲疾呼，實行對意制裁。法國既然也同是國聯的支持者，當然不便公然離開日內瓦，明白贊助意大利的侵略行為；但為了防禦德國，法意曾簽定了羅馬協定，在巴黎外交家的內心中自然也不願拋開自己這個新的友好，為人作嫁，而眼隨在英人之後，以對付意大利；因此，在矛盾中，法國對意阿問題便採取了緩和的企圖兩全的態度。它一面和英國在日內瓦不斷談判，表面尊重國聯盟約，一面父向羅馬暗送秋波，表示它不願積極實行制裁。這樣一來，當然會使英帝國主義大為不快，但除了不快之外，一時也並沒有積極的對付辦法；而且，因為另外沒有好的友伴，還不得不裝着笑臉繼續與馬巴黎交談，夢想英法關係能在一致對意下和好起來。　　同時，正在英意衝突尖銳，英法不能一致的時候，霹靂一聲，在上月七日希特勒突然宜布廢除諾加羅公的，進兵萊茵河地帶，並提出意見六點，以作國際和平談判之基礎。他的藉口是法國與蘇聯訂立互助公的，已經是違反了諾加羅條的的精神，所以這條的可無須遵守，而德軍開入萊茵區是正當的。這對於法國簡直是一種公然進攻的挑戰行為。因此，法人對於希特勒這種毀的行為的回答，除了調集軍隊開往邊境布防外，也就跑到日內瓦去高呼萊茵河畔的危機，要求諾加羅公的簽的國和國聯制裁德國。但這時侵阿的意軍已進到查那湖地域了，英國正睜着眼注視它在尼羅河上的權利，對於法國要求的答覆則是要它更注意東菲的戰爭，說東非問題未解决以前，歐洲安全無法維持。當法國和平方案提出時，柏林方面認為是「高聳雲宵之大廈」，日內瓦認為是「幻想的野心的，莫可實施的」，倫敦的態度也是非常冷淡。本月十八日英首相鮑爾溫在華塞特發表演說，除猛烈攻擊意大利外，更公然謂希特勒有「撥開全歐陰霾之最大權力。」這種情形當然是法國所大不高興的。但為了對付德國，為了不致使英人公然扶助希將勒的毀約行為，它仍不得不繼續與倫敦談判，要求英國的軍事援助。雖然英法乃至比利時的外交家和參謀部為了萊茵河畔問題的不斷談判，並沒有商討出有效的辦法，但外交談判仍是要進行的，因為他們雖然各有懷抱，在目前情形下雖然合不起來，但彼此卻也不願一下就分手的。　　因為芙法關係的貌合神離，莫索里尼和希特勒這兩大野心家當然更可大瞻地在他們的胃險途徑上賽跑了。事實上，因為有法國在日內瓦緩和制裁空氣，侵阿意軍不僅不停止進攻，而且不顧一切地使用毒瓦斯，以毒殺手無寸鐵的阿國人民。現在意軍已佔領台西，進逼阿京了，尼羅河上的英闕權利巳感到了更現實的威脅，英意衝突已發展到了更直接的情勢，但這除使大英帝國的神經緊張外，巴黎方面對這種情形仍是保持其安閑態度。在另一方面，希特勒在造成了德軍開入萊茵河畔的事實後，更進而在那里努力建設防防御工程，並表示將收回已失的殖民地；同時還提出了許多新的建議，新的問題，以投台倫敦的希求，企圖將西歐的視綫轉向東歐去。道種表現當然不會移　英國注視尼羅河的視綫，但對於巴黎卻算忍無可忍受的進攻。所以，法國在英人優容希特勒的毀約行為下，最近甚至有單獨自由行動的表示。目前日內瓦對於尼羅河與萊茵河的問題都非常注意，但這注意力一是來自倫敦，一是來自巴黎。因此，在目前日內瓦也就有兩種制裁的呼聲：一是加緊制裁意大早，一是實行制裁德國。主張前者的不消說是英國，但法國卻在從中緩和，反之，主張後者的是法國，但英國卻在勸巴黎的政治家不要「意氣用事」。　　據本月二十一日報載，艾登彭古談話結果，英法已相互讓步，成立妥協。在這妥協中，艾登所得的是：「　法國務勿意氣用事，循至一怒面退出國聯，蓋國聯會雖無力解决萊茵河問題，但法國苟與國聯會絕裾，則尼難河問題將愈感棘手也。　法國對於現行各項對意制裁辦法，務勿取消，其於國聯會盟約亦當癢續信守之。　關於萊茵河問題，英國當與德國進行談判，俾將德法兩國所提之和平計劃同時加以考慮；但為國務當假以時日，俾英國得以從容進行。「至於彭古所得的，則是。「　出行各項對意制裁辦法雖可予以維持，但不必再事加緊。　英國對於萊茵河事件，與意阿爭端務當一視同仁，母得軒輊，以免增長德國之氣燄，血致再作破壞條約之舉動，而意國亦不致快快觖望，則以　國對於歐洲集體安全組織，刻已準備重行參加也。　關於意阿爭端，英法兩國政府務當精誠合作，以覓求和平解决方案。」這樣的所謂妥協，在表面上雖然表現出了英法兩國相互的關心，所謂「友善精神」，但在實際上法國並未拋開意大利，積極幫助英國；同樣，英國也未放棄優容希特勒的態度，與法國站在一邊堅决施行國際條約的義務。事實上，就在這項所謂妥協成立後的第一天，在國聯行政院會議中英法代表的意見也有顯著的不一致，囚而使國聯的結構露出「裂痕」。據艾登的演說，則是意大利違反國聯盟約，應該一致對付；但彭古則謂要對付歐洲方面之威脅，必須意國通力合作。—這種表現已經充分說明了所謂英法的妥恊只是到某種程度為止的，而且是表面的；倫敦與巴黎的精神，到現在為止，都還談不到一致。　　但是，在這樣貌合神離的英法關係下，第一必會使德意更大膽地向危險道上邁進，因而引起英意以及法德的衝突史加尖銳。現在，意軍已佔領了界在英埃蘇丹的高伯拉等地域，與英國駐在該處的陸空軍遙遙相對，因之英意的武裝衝突大有一觸即發之勢。至於德法的關係，雖不一定有很决爆發戰爭的可能，但在英國的優容和鼓勵之下，希特勒的不斷冒險行動隨時都有可能點燃歐洲的火綫的。其次，由於英法的不能一致，國際聯盟今後將更要成為不能解决問題的無用機關，歐洲乃至世界局勢將要更加混亂。　　同時，繼德國宣布廢除諾加羅公約之後的，還有　匈的軍備重整　擴充，土耳其的恢復海峽軍備，這些都足以使歐洲局勢更加緊張和混亂的。單就現在英法德意四大國間之關係及這裹所舉出的新的事件看來，我們就很担心和　之神的壽命是要能維持到一九三七年了！介紹「結婚指導」　　「飲食男女，人之大欲。」「男女居室，人之大倫。」所以男女結婚，為人生應做的事。但是社會上為什麼常常發生一種不安現象呢？像早婚·晚婚·私婚·逃婚·離婚·重婚·失戀自殺·三角戀愛等等事情，這都是沒有人來公開講過。學校裏沒有專門科目，學術團體少公開講演，父母不多指導。現在好了，有劉麟生瞿紹伊等七位專家合著了一本「結婚指導」，從各方面來指導結婚，凡男女靑年均應人手一編。該書由上海四馬路二七七號動奮書局出版，定價每冊七角，特價四角，以一月為限云。碎錦凱羅紀伯倫（Kahlil　Gibran）嘉言綠  劉楊朱　　在你不安於你的思想的時候，你就說話，在你不能再在你心的孤寂中生活的時候，你就要在你的唇上生活，而聲音是一種消遣，一種娛樂，在你許多的談話裏，思想半受殘害。—談話　　我能談你們的善性，卻不能談惡性。因為什麼是惡，不只是靑被他自身的飢渴所困苦麼？的確底，有善飢餓的時候，他肯向黑暗中覓食，渴的時候他也肯喝死水。—談善惡　　常常在你拒絕逸樂的時候，你只是把慾望收藏在你心身的隱處。誰知道在今日似乎避免了的事情，等到明日不會再浮現麼？連你的身體都知道他的遺傳興正當的需要而不肯被欺騙。—談逸樂　　只在你們從沉默的河中啜飲時，才眞能歌唱。只在你們達到山巔時，你們才開始攀援。只在大地索取你四肢時，你們才眞正的跳舞。—談死　　愛雖給你加冠，他也要釘你在十字架，他雖栽焙你，也剎剪你。—談愛　　你們的孩子都不是你們的孩子，乃是生命為自己所渴望的兒女。他們是借你們而來，卻不是從你們而來，他們雖和你們同在，卻不屬於你們。你們可以給他們以愛，卻不能給他們以思想，因為他們有自己的思想。—談孩子　　你把你的產業給人，那只算給了一點，當你以身佈施的時侯，那才是眞正的施與。—談施與　　生命的確是黑暗的，除非是有了激勵，一切的激勵都是盲目的，除非是有了知識，一切的知識都是徒然的，除非是有了工作，一切的工作都是虛空的，除非是有了愛。當你仁愛地工作的時候，你便與自己與人類，與上帝連繁為一。—談工作　　你的衣服掩蓋了許多的美，卻隱不住醜惡。你們雖在衣服裏可尋得隱秘的自由，卻也尋得橛飾與羈勒了。—談衣服　　你們是道，也是行道的人。當你們中有人跌倒的時候，他是為了他後面的人而跌倒，是一塊絆腳石的警吿。是的，他也為他前面的人而跌倒，因為他們的步履雖然又快又穩，卻沒有把那絆腳石挪開。—談罪與罰　　你們中如有人要審判一個不忠誠的妻子，讓他也拿天平來秤一秤她丈夫的心，拿尺來量一量他的靈魂。讓鞭撻擾人者的人先察一察那被擾者的靈性。—談罪與罰　　你們這些願持公正的法官，你們怎樣裁判那忠誠共外而盜竊其中的人？你們又將怎樣刑罰一個肉體受戮，而在他自已是心靈遭減的人？你們又將怎樣控吿那在行為上是刁猾，暴戾，而在事實上也是被威逼被虐待的人呢？—談罪與罰　　你們喜歡立法，卻也更喜歡犯法。如同那在海濱游戲的孩子，勤懇的建造了沙塔，然後又嘻笑的將他毀壞。—談法律　　你的心靈常常是戰塲，在戰塲上，你的理性與判斷和你的熱情與嗜慾開戰。我恨不能在你的心靈中作一個調停者，依我可以讓你們心中分子從爭競與釁隙變成合一與和鳴。—談理性與熱情外埠郵政代辦所鴉片的種植和吸用  綏人　　綏遠歸綏通訊　　近年來嚴厲禁毒的結果，內地各省都有相當的成效了。但在邊遠的省份以及有特殊關係的地方，因為種種的牽制，有的根本上無法禁止，有的只能在某種限度上加以禁止。在綏遠就是這種情形，雖然對於毒品中最劇烈的白麵白丸等嚴厲地禁止販賣和吸用，但於鴉片烟的種植和吸用則是公開的，或者說是官家所允許的。　　這個地方因為接近沙漢，牠的氣候是非常惡劣，而土地更是異常貧瘠的。一年四季是冷的早暖的晚，大部份的時間不能生長任何植物。而土地則是荒原無垠，耕作困難，因此，一般人民就都認種植鴉片為有利可圖了。　　種植鴉片也和種植其他植物一樣，是在春暖時下種，在夏來秋初時收穫。只要在道個期間不遇到塞外特有的冰雹，暴風，酷旱以及在收耯時的陰雨連綿，鴉片便可得到豐收了。　　鴉片的種籽分作兩種，一種是單頭，一種是複頭。單頭是一株鴉片只開一朶花，結一個粟頭。複頭是開幾朶花，結幾個栗頭。粟頭的多少雖然不同，但對於烟量的生產上並無多大影響。據有經騐的人說，複頭反不如單頭的生產量多。因為複頭生的粟頭既多，其體積也就小，所含的烟量也就少了。　　鴉片種植的方法，雖然與一　　物一樣，是按時下種，施肥料，芟草等，但為增加烟量，也用盡種種人工的力量。在田地中有水井，或因種烟而掘有水井的，大半用種植菜園和培餐花圃的方法來經營。他們在田地中築成許　菜畦和小的水道，除了施肥料，芟草外，天如不雨，則每日汲水灌溉。因此烟苗都長得異常肥大，烟的出產量當然也就因之增加了。這種叫做水烟。還有一種早烟，是與種核普通穀物一樣的，其所需的水量不能山人工來帮助，只有聽天由命。不過，水烟並不普遍。因在一般的田地中，掘井，灌溉需要很大的人力與財力，一般的農民大都負擔不起。只有靠近城市的菜園能從事水烟的種植。　　在每年的六七月之間，罌粟花便滿山遍野的開了。肥嫩的綠葉上托着紅白黃紫的美麗花朵。把這荒涼遼闊的原野頓時變成了美好的花園。罌票花的美麗，單從「阿芙蓉」這個別名上就可以知道了。在顏色和花的形式上，無論是單瓣或複辦，都興芙蓉完全一樣，只是稍微小點罷了。誰也想不到，這樣美艷的花竟會產生那種把人類毀家滅身的果呢！　　鴉片的收穫期是在七月的後牛月。在這時最要緊的是要天氣晴朗。因為在這時陽光越晒着栗頭，則割出的烟漿便也越多。如果在割烟的幾天遇上陰雨速綿的天氣，那烟的收穫就要大　减色了。　　因為割烟的期間只有很短促的幾天，所以必須多僱日工。這些日工又大都是癮君子，因此，於工資之外，必須加送少許烟膏，作為他們臨時過癮之用。割烟時，每人手執鐵形小刀一柄和圓形鐵盒一個。繞粟頭圍割一週，烟漿即隨之冒出，然後抹於鐵盒中。要是鐵盒滿了，便把牠集中到大的鐵橋裹。割烟也需要相當的技術和熟練，因為割的太深了或太淺了都要影響到烟的出產量的。　　鴉片收割完成之後，有的出售烟漿，有的把烟漿曝成烟土之後纔去出售。一般窮苦的農民大部份都是倫偷模摸地出售烟漿。因為他們在苛捐雜稅，高利貸的重壓之下，决沒有從容的時閒把牠晒成烟土之後再去出售的，而偷偷地出售烟漿，對於他們還可以省下一層烟土稅的剝削。　　此地所生產的鴉片，除了本地的居民消費一部份外，大部份都集中在此地所特有的烟土販的手裹。他們在此地設立烟土莊，從事收買，然後再推銷到別省去。本省烟土主要的銷塲是山西。因山西於嚴厲禁止白麵，白丸的吸用與販賣後，就實行鴉片公賣。最近因華北的特殊情形，平津也成了此地烟土的大好銷售市塲了。　　鴉片的價格在此地大的在大約一元到一元五角左右。最　的特候也不過兩元。普通零售，五分錢就可以買到些許的烟膏。　　吸用鴉片在此地是公開的。除了娼竂和供公眾吸用的烟館之外，大部份的居民都有這種嗜好。在交際塲中，鴉片烟也就成了主要的應酬工具。如果有客人來拜訪而不請他吸「洋烟」（本地人稱鴉片烟為洋烟），還無疑地是很失鱟面的。一般居民還有一種可怕的觀念，就是吸用「洋烟」是表示你時髦，闊綽，否則，就覺得你是很寒酸似的。　　此地的烟館開設得非常的多。每條街上總有兩三家。凡門首懸有　　記的字號和玻璃窗內擺著烟罐及小秤的，都是烟館。烟館一方面售贊烟膏，一方　燈供給吸用。一間黑暗的小屋內，在這塞外特有的大土坑上，經常的橫陳着三五個　君人在吞雲吐霧。　　在這樣的環境中，一般小有產的居民有這種嗜好，原不足為奇。最可驚的是在很多的貧民和乞丐中，也染有這種嗜好。在歸綏縣政府的附近，有一家貧民。一個母親和兩個兒子都有鴉片癮。兩個兒子是以縫鞋為業，每日的牧入不過三幾角錢。以這樣的收人而染有嗜好，所以時常沒有飯吃。乞丐在討得食物之後，還常聽見他喊出：「給點烟灰吧！給點烟灰吧！」的呼聲。可見鴉片烟在此地為害之烈了。　　在鴉片烟的種植，販賣，吸用上，形成一筆很大的稅收。因為種植鴉片，有所謂烟畝罰欵。販責，必須貼禁烟局的印花。吸用，又須納烟燈捐。烟畝罰欵在每年烟苗生出之後，由禁烟局派員會同各縣勘定丈量。因為水早烟的產量不同，罰欵的數目也因之而異。水烟的數目一般比旱烟多三分之一。烟燈捐普通的吸戶是沒有的。只有以營業為件質的烟館和娼寮纔繳納。烟館大半是每月五元。娼寮則分三等，最高的也是五元。烟土稅是由禁烟局發賣印花，按照烟土的重量，在販賣時加貼。要則便以私土沒收。　　在此地一時不能澈底禁烟，大概也是因稅收的關係。在道地瘠民貧的半沙漢地方，面積雖然較北方的任何省分為大，但人民稀少，毫無工商業可言，財政上的困難是任何省分所沒有的。所以，多年以來，就不得不靠這筆稅收，作為重要的挹注。　　從去年以來，地方政府會曾公佈分區禁種，限期烟民登記的辦法，打算從種植和吸用兩方面逐滿禁絕。但從財政上和目前華北的特殊關係上看來，這恐怕只是一種不能推行的官樣文章罷了。藝壇「再世復仇記」觀後感  立箴　　美國影片的特色仍舊在這一張片子里反映出來。　　小市民們看膩了大腿粉臂，自然得找另一種刺激，於是所謂恐怖影片少不得也走上了時運。推測其社會意義，還是與劍俠影片同共源流的。　　所謂「恐怕之王」卡洛夫主演的「再世復仇記」它是利用了所謂科學的進步，假設一個新的因果循環，用報復主義來發洩一個仇敵的警恨，所以這張影片可以說是最合我們中國民族「惡有惡報，善有善報」的傳統迷信，而使老太太，老太爺，甚至準老太太，準老太爺的小姐公子們看了大快人心而感到科學力量之偉大的。　　故事是這樣的：有梅力脫及屈格者，因犯案恐馬頓吐露眞情，與兩個操權舞彝的律師諾倫和羅德商議，定計先殺法官以期報復。恰巧埃爾門（卡洛夫飾）方出獄，苦無職業，屈格就詭稱法官的妻疑法官有外遇，要雇人窺伺法官的行動。埃爾門信以為眞，每晚在法官門外徘徊。一天，屈格等暗殺了法官，卽將屍移於埃爾門的車上，結果埃爾門被誣為兇手，判電刑處死。這一件事發生的當時，適為祁美與南茜所目睹，聞埃氏被處死刑，不忍坐視，遂據實告發，迨審判長電止行刑，巳不及了。埃氏雖死，終為科學家布門博士用最新科學方法將埃氏施救復活，但復活後，記憶力已失去，而友仇卻仍能判別，結果梅力脫和屈格兩人遭埃氏殺害，諾倫與羅德亦因再殺埃氏在飛逃時車撞燈桿而死。　　這故事的空想不實當然不容諱言，尤以科學能使人再生這一點更見荒唐。不過「法律吃人」卻給了一個深刻的描寫，我們不難由此推想，人類自有所謂法律以來，也不知有多少生命斷送於這一個名詞之下了！　　本來世界上有的是冤枉，沈冤莫白的事是早經司空見慣了的，但淺薄的報復思想就如「再世復仇記」所開列給我們的方式進行了。這又好像為的是要懲戒一般作惡多端的人的；因為他們對於過去的「果報」的思想已失去駕馭的力量了一，所以「新的果報說」說：「你們不能再作惡了，將來科學進步以後，任何惡人都難逃恢恢的天網的，猶如梅力股·屈格·諾倫和羅德。可不是嗎？他們不是終於都證了因果了嗎？」名人傳記幾個重要的探險家  泳石　　隨若產業的發展，文藝復興時代的出現，自由研究精神的發達，在十四世紀以後的西歐出現了各種的發明和發見。如時計，眼鏡，火藥，磁石，印刷術　　以下接第五版

等，都是這時代的重要發明。但在這些發明中，對於近代文明影響最大的，要算火藥和印刷術以及磁石三者。因為有了火藥，舊有的封建時代的武器和戰術才為之一變，武士的勢力也因之衰落；有了印刷術，近代文化才得大大的發展：而磁石的發現更使航海者敢在沒有星光的黑夜里大膽遠航，刺激了航海業的進步，因而刺激了產業和科學的發達。　　我們所要在這見介紹的與近代歷史有密切關係的幾位重要探險家，便是在近代文明開始的時期中，在磁石的發現和航海的發達的條件下出現的人物。　　英國發展新大陸的開端者加波特歐洲白人在北美勢力最大的要算英國人：差不多除南部一帶以外，所有這地方都滿印着英人的足跡。所以北美有「盎格魯撒克遜亞美利加」之稱。但英國發展新大陸的開端者則是的翰·加波特（John，Cabot　一四五〇——一四九八）。　　加波特在一四五〇年生於意大利的斐勒加，但他卻是侍奉英王亨利七世的船戶。就在哥倫布從橫斷大西洋的壯舉歸來的四年之後，在一四九七年，加波特即和他的兒子率同十八個部下，乘着小船馬休號出帆布列士特，發見了新的航路。　　他駕着小舟，乘風破浪，右三個月的危險的航海之後，到達了拉布刺達半島沿岸。那時他還以為自己到了中國；但他考察的結果，沒有發見繁華的都市，沒有什麼文明表現，這樣才迷惑起來，使他對這地方發生了不可思議的戚覺　　這惱時候，英國資本主義已在開始發展了，找殖民地的欲求，正在它心中成長。所以，加波特發現北美拉布刺達半島後，他即在英王的名字下佔領了這塊土地。從此英吉利王旗便開始在這荒島上飄揚，後來這地方便成為了不列顚帝國的殖民地。　　加波特從拉布刺達歸來，沿途差不一多行了一千哩的探險，在這年的八月六一日才算安抵布列士特港。他這次探險的成功，英王當然非常高興，除特別嘉獎他外，並給了他許多金錢和船隻，並派了很多的人充他的部下，命他再去探險。於是，在次年五月他又同他的見子率領眾人遠航，結果到達了北美的基沙皮克灣。但這里也沒有黃金，寶石，象牙等物，也是荒涼之地，所以他們很是失望，只得再行歸來。　　但是，這次安然歸來的只有加波特的兒子的船，其他的都不知道漂流到何處去了。因此，開於加波特的消息從此也就湮沒無聞。　　自此以後，英國人有一個很長久的時間沒有十分注意到新大陸：他們在北美的發展乃是較後的事。但不管怎樣，加波特的探險總算是英國殖民北美的先聲。　　法國開拓新大陸的先驅維拉扎羅果凡尼·達·維拉扎羅（Giovanni　da　Terrazano一四八〇——一五二七）本來也是意大利人，他的誕生地是弗羅倫斯，但因他久在法蘭西生活，所以他探險的成續也就是法國的了。　　一五二四年，維拉扎羅率領五十人西向大西洋航行，在羅斯加羅利那的沙嘴邊發見了陸地。當下他便在非常高與中，在他的隨身日記上寫着：此處是前人未到的新陸地。　　從此他更續往南行，經通一些時間後，更折向北進，途中他發見了許多港灣，就中之一便是紐約灣。在這里他看到了哈德孫河口，引起了他特別的注意，並預見了今日紐約市的發展。本來，這哈德孫河的名稱是由此後再發見它的亨利·哈德孫所給的，但事實上維拉扎羅的發見是在先此的八十五年。　　隨後維拉扎羅繼續航行，到達了諾凡新戈夏半島，知道了加拿大。這便是後來法人佔領加拿大的根據。　　為西班牙征服墨西哥的可爾特斯當西班牙發展的時候，差不多美洲大部都是它的屬地；墨西哥當然也是其中之一。但最先由探險而征服墨西哥的，乃是在十六世紀初的西班牙軍人赫爾蘭德·可爾特斯（Hernando　Cortes　一四八五——一五四七）。　　在一五一九年二月，有一隊西班牙軍人聽到在西方有金鑛豐饒的陸地；這些靑年軍人素富冒險性，所以他們聽到這消息後，馬上就由一位隊長率領到這產金地去探險。這位隊長，便是可爾特斯。　　可爾特斯率領的一隊西班牙靑年軍人由古巴島出帆，在現今的委拉古魯斯市上陸，向着現在的墨西哥市前進。在上陸時，他曾用「破釜沈舟」的辦法，把他們所乘的船破壞，向隊員們表示不進即死的决心。這樣，在三個月之後，他們終於到達了其所希望的黃金都市墨西哥。　　但是，這黃金都市中住的有墨西哥土人，他們有組織，有領袖，遠來的西班牙人不易進去。因此可爾特斯便用詭計，把墨西哥士人首領虜獲，並突向失掉首領的士人進攻，終於把這黃金都市征服了。從此墨西哥市和其附近的地方都為西班牙所佔據，它的領土便擴大到新大陸了。　　隨後，他們又聽到鬨都拉斯有富饒的鑛產，並在那里有到太平洋的海峽，因之在一五二四年可爾特斯又從墨西哥市出發，經過三千哩的遠征後，更到達了鬨都拉斯灣；由此又乘船繼續前進，直到了茲爾基羅。這個地方便是以後往中美探險的新的出發點。科學業話  諒殺人光線　　所謂殺人光綫，是英人格林特爾·馬休斯發明的。他之開始公開研究這種前所未聞的怪光錢，是在一千九百十五年，即是在距今二十年以前的時侯。　　馬休斯研究死光，曾得到了英政府的一二五，〇〇〇圓的補助金。自他實行奇異的實騐以來，一向世界各國都沒有人發表關於研究這怪光綫的何等的報吿，所以這光綫一時間在名實上都成為了英國獨佔研究的東西。　　英政府對於這個怪光錢的研究，不知什麼緣故，簡直是極蓋保護的能事。他們在維爾士山地上建築了近代的科學魔城，周圍都張着通電流的鐵條，在四方還裝置着不可視的光錢，這位科學家馬休斯便件在這樣的科學魔城中，與世隔絕，專心地去研究他那殺人光綫。他這樣苦心的研究不僅犧牲畢生的精神，而且是賭着生命的，因為在這能殺人的光錢之研究中，在這樣的科學魔城內，偶一不愼，也有可能將自己殺死的。　　馬休斯的研究雖然很秘密，但當此各國都在拚命準備殺人大戰的時候，別的科學家也會想到如何利用光綫來殺人的。因此，在他的研究之後，別的國家的科學者也實行了並不劣於他的研究。如大家所知道的，美國電氣學者特斯拉所研究的怪光錢能殺死數英里之外的兔；如意大利馬可尼及德國杜尼可斯基等現刻也正一在秘密研究怪光綫，其研究到底進展到了什麼程度，外人雖不得而知，但總可預料那也必然是殺人利器吧。　　同時，在最近，克路加博士更發現了比從來的X光綫還要強十六倍的不可視的怪力光綫。這個怪力光綫由其放射機放射出來，可以殺傷五十米突以外的生物。據檢查，那被照射的生物，在其血球中的白血球是被減少了八十分之三或二十分之一。而且，依克略加博士的實騐，這光綫的放射機如隱蔽在地下，那在這附近是任何人都不能接近的。此外如戰車等的司機人，這光錢也可以把他射殺。　　這樣，所謂殺人光錢的出現，已經成為事實了；而且這光錢的種類還很多，現在誰也猜不透就中要算那一種最為厲害。文藝作品少女的母性（四）  少雄　　她巴不得那小的孩子除了喂乳和更換尿屎布的時候之外，老是不聲不響的睡在床上。可是這也不好：這孩子白天裏睡眠過度了，晚上便要不時的醒來，捧頭縮腳的啼哭着，吵得要給他伴睡的母親夜間不得安眠，白天裹做事沒有精神，使她的工作又無形地受了損失。至於大的孩子，她更是希望他能跟着雲蓮整天在屋子外玩耍，只要不闖禍，不和別的孩子們鬧事就好。她常常慫恿着他說：　　『乖囝囝，你很乖的，你到雲蓮那裹去玩。過一歇，等媽媽賺了錢買糖給你吃。」　　不過，這也有例外。如果這孩子在外面玩得過久了，她又要記掛他了。　　是一個星期日的上午，這男女兩主人在樓上一間兼充書室的臥房裹，面對面的坐在寫字檯旁，合譯着一部英文小字典。書局限他們於兩月內交稿，眼見得一個月已過去，而譯文還沒有完成一半，因此工作頓形緊張而忙碌起來。這時，小的孩子正展開着四肢，安然地酣睡着，全身在床上排成了一個大而潦草的「太」字；那大的孩子也出去玩了。室內的空氣像死一般的岑寂：有時夫婦偶然說一兩句閒話，或妻子遇字典中有些疑難的字句，要求丈夫解答，除此以外，差不多只有查詢英漢字典時翻動書頁的聲音，以及鋼筆沙沙地在紙上移動着的聲音。　　突然間，小的孩子醒了，兩手捧着頭部，兩腿懸空的蜷曲着，用力地伸了一個懶腰，接着便是啼哭。女主人的心怔了一怔，但仍不動聲色似的寫着她的東西。　　孩子哭得更利害了，聲音忽而急促而緊張，忽而又拖長得像透不出氣的樣子。她皺了一下眉，可是依然沒有想抱他的意思。　　孩子的哭已堅持了四五分鐘，聲音仍是那麼的大，好像永不會停息似的，同時，這哭聲裏似乎也含有悲哀的成分和反抗的意味。那個平素對孩子漠然不甚關心的男主人，到這時也有些不忍起來。　　『孩子在哭呢！」他對妻子說，意思是要她去抱，但他自己卻並不動手，好像抱撫孩子只是女人範圍內的事。　　『雲蓮買紙烟去了，馬上就回來的，讓她去抱罷。她非常喜歡抱孩子。……讓他哭一會，不要緊的。』她坦然的說。　　果然，女主人說完了話，剛提着鋼筆去濡墨水時，就聽得樓下開門的聲音　　『來了！來了！』雲蓮纔踏上樓梯，便這麼熱情地呌喊着，無疑地，她巳聽見了孩子的哭聲了。於是她就迅速地上樓。把買來物事和餘錢交給了女主人，雲蓮就走到床前，把孩子擊舉起來，一面向他裝着哭臉，調弄他說：　　「呵！這樣苦呀！這樣可憐呀！傷心呢！」　　孩子的哭本來巳預備靜止了，經她這麼一說，彷彿是觸動了悲懷，又傷着嘴臉，哀哀地哭起來了。（未完）播音特別節目　　麗琳社　　中西（一〇四〇）上午十一時至十二時　　前奏曲（口琴劍秋）人面桃花（麗娟）夜深深（麗琳）休息五分鐵（麗麗）警變（麗琦）太平花（麗娜）我不能忘記您（麗娟）好妹妹（麗琳）愛向何處零（麗麗）鋤頭舞歌（劍秋）　　雷電劇社話劇　　李樹德（九四〇）中午零時三刻至一時半　　「南歸」　　領導：陳奕　　播演者：金儀，林蜚，馬翎，董偉。　　月星歌詠社　　利利（一二四〇）下午二時至三時　　新鳳陽歌（張偉）小天使（夏斐）新鳳求鳳佩雯）永遠在後台（　玲）新夜來香（梁嫣國花（茉茜）城市之光（莉茜）燕雙飛（莉潔）娘子軍（張偉）賣花女（茉茜）等一等吧（璐玲）（莉潔）春潮回來吧（施蘊）（佩雯）鋤頭舞歌（全體）　　鮑明 1936.04.26

Arita Hosts Foreign Journalists, Explains Japanese Diplomacy, Implements Peaceful Policies Towards China and Russia, and Requests Freedom of Trade with Britain and the United States 1

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita, at 3:30 PM on the 25th, met with foreign news reporters at his official residence to elaborate on the Japanese government's diplomatic policies. The Director of the Information Department, Amau, was also present. The Foreign Minister then engaged in a question-and-answer session with the reporters, explaining specific policies until 5 PM. The contents of the diplomatic policies expressed by the Foreign Minister to the reporters are as follows:

Japan's diplomatic policy, as elucidated in the Imperial Rescript issued by the Emperor upon Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, remains unchanged to this day. We aim to stabilize East Asia, foster close relations with friendly nations, and contribute to world peace and human happiness. There have always been numerous methods advocated and implemented for the maintenance of world peace, but none have proven fully effective. We firmly believe that nations should eliminate the root causes threatening peace and make their best efforts to maintain peace within their capabilities. For Japan, the stabilization of East Asia is a matter of national survival and a divinely bestowed responsibility to the world. To fulfill this weighty responsibility, it is necessary to establish good neighborly relations with neighboring countries, namely China and Russia, with "Manchukuo" at the center, to stabilize the overall situation.

Recently, as a result of frequent disputes in the areas bordering Manchuria, Russia, and Mongolia, various rumors have spread in Europe and America. However, we will never initiate illegal acts of aggression unless provoked by hostile actions. There are currently various pending issues between the Soviet Union and Japan-Manchukuo. We believe these issues can be resolved amicably through diplomatic negotiations. China and Japan, sharing the same script and ethnicity, have a relationship akin to lips and teeth. It goes without saying that the primary goal of both countries is to coexist and prosper together. However, as the two countries are neighbors, various problems naturally arise, which is unavoidable. But we sincerely hope that the two major friendly nations of East Asia will cooperate closely to ensure peace in East Asia. In Europe and America, some people often criticize Japan's policy towards China with malicious intent. However, if these countries were to stand in Japan's position and face the actual situation squarely, they would surely understand our attitude.

We also constantly strive to improve relations with Britain, the United States, and other countries in other aspects, paying particular attention to relations with countries around the Pacific Ocean. Recently, conflicts of interest in trade and commerce have been observed between Japan and these countries. However, these are not insurmountable if appropriate adjustments are made from a standpoint of mutual dependence. At this juncture, to revitalize the world economy and promote international peace, we propose to restore freedom of trade and foster an atmosphere of freedom and trust internationally. This will undoubtedly make a great contribution to human well-being and prosperity. (Telegraph from Allied Press, 25th)

Arita Says No Need to Conclude Non-Aggression Pact Proposed by Soviet Russia 2

(Tokyo) After Foreign Minister Arita elaborated on diplomatic policies to foreign news reporters, the foreign reporters raised various questions. The following is a record of the questions and answers between the reporters and the Foreign Minister.

Some in America are concerned about the occurrence of a Russo-Japanese war. What is your view?

The current situation has not reached the point of war. It is also possible that Europe and America are exaggerating the facts and spreading rumors.

Is a Russo-Japanese war impossible?

Napoleon once said, "The word 'impossible' is not in my dictionary."

Are Russo-Japanese relations worse than they were several years ago?

There are now more pending issues than before, and there have been an increase of incidents such as border issues.

Does Japan intend to conclude a Russo-Japanese non-aggression treaty?

In 1932, when Ambassador Yoshizawa, stationed in France, was returning to Japan, Foreign Minister Litvinov of the Soviet Union made this proposal when he passed through Moscow. However, it was rejected because the timing was premature. Japan proposed to Russia to handle border disputes and establish a border demarcation committee, which would have a greater effect in practice. Japan continues to pursue negotiations based on this policy today.

The Soviet Union is increasing its military buildup in the Far East. Does Japan intend to demand that the Soviet Union reduce its Far Eastern forces to an equal level with Japan's?

Japan is quite concerned about the Soviet Union maintaining an excessive military presence in the Far East. Reducing Soviet military buildup would alleviate the atmosphere between the two countries, which everyone recognizes. However, Japan has never made the withdrawal or reduction of the Soviet Far Eastern Army a subject of negotiations with Russia.

What impact does the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance treaty have on Japan's diplomacy towards Russia?

Although France has stated that this treaty does not extend to the Far East, some observers in Japan believe that the Soviet Union, having obtained security guarantees for its western borders through the treaty, will be able to devote its remaining resources to strengthening its influence in the Far East in the future.

Rumors of a Secret Japanese-German Pact, Some Enthusiastic About It 3

Does Japan intend to conclude a Japanese-German alliance to counter the Franco-Soviet treaty?

Some people in Japan are enthusiastically advocating for Japanese-German cooperation, but the government authorities have not considered this issue.

Japan's So-Called Three Principles Towards China, Arita Says to Implement Its Spirit 4

You served as Ambassador to China and met with Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Qun in Nanjing. What was the impact?

The purpose of my talks with the Nanjing leadership was to deepen mutual understanding, not to conduct formal negotiations on a specific topic. Therefore, I cannot speak of its concrete effects. However, based on the impression I received from this meeting, there are many difficulties ahead for China and Japan, and a great deal of effort is needed.

Will Japan proceed with negotiations with China based on the so-called three principles?

I am determined to inherit the policies of former Foreign Minister Hirota and to realize Sino-Japanese cooperation in the spirit of the three principles.

Will the three principles be applied through coercive means or through a method of mutual concession?

There is no need for a coercive policy. It goes without saying that mutual peaceful means should be used to gradually increase the density of cooperation between the two countries. (Telegraph from Allied Press, 25th)

General Supervisor Chiang Issues Order to Seriously Investigate and Register Opium Smokers 8

Ensuring that there are no omissions or false reports after this investigation.

(Nanjing) General Supervisor Chiang issued an order to the provincial and municipal governments and the special commissioners for prohibition in each province on the 25th to supervise and urge a serious investigation and registration of opium smokers, ensuring that there are no omissions or false reports, and to prepare a report for verification. The original order stated that the purpose of this investigation and registration of opium smokers is, on the one hand, to obtain the accurate number of smokers to serve as a standard for establishing opium addiction treatment centers and implementing phased treatment based on age, and, on the other hand, to obtain the accurate total amount smoked by all smokers to serve as a basis for unified management and allocation of supply and demand, ensuring that the established method of gradual reduction year by year is followed until prohibition is achieved, and there is no room for carelessness or perfunctoriness, and any omissions. However, opium smokers in various places may not understand the government's policies and intentions, and often hide and do not register due to overly strict suppression, or even if they register and obtain a license, they do not report the true amount smoked, or they report more than they smoke, or even report less than they smoke. Although this is generally due to the smokers' concealment and fear, hoping to evade punishment, the responsible officials of governments at all levels should also supervise and urge personnel at all levels to conduct serious investigations and practical inspections, ensuring that there are no omissions or false reports after this investigation, so that the promotion of the prohibition policy can be completed as scheduled. All those who are registered as smokers and the amount they reported should be compiled in a statistical table of the number of registered smokers in accordance with Article 7 of the investigation method after the completion of the process and submitted for review. The statistical table is now issued, and two copies should be prepared and submitted within half a month by the provincial and municipal governments together with the special commissioners to compile two copies of the summary table, one to be transferred to this General Supervision Office for verification and one to be submitted to the provincial and municipal governments for review and inspection for management purposes. (Telegraph from Central News Agency, 25th)

Current Affairs Commentary

Flood Prevention During the Peach Blossom Flood Season 20

— Du

Our country has suffered from floods year after year, which has almost become a common occurrence. The severity of the disaster last year was far beyond comparison with the past. The two major river systems in the north and south competed to flood, echoing each other. The vastness of the affected area and the duration of the disaster directly exhausted those engaged in disaster relief. Not to mention the material losses, from the perspective of the value of life, countless people were swallowed by the floodwaters and buried in the stomachs of fish, countless people floated and sank, becoming companions of the waves, countless people were displaced and unable to find shelter, and countless people were infected with plagues and had no one to tell. Outside the disaster-stricken areas, some people worked tirelessly to engage in relief efforts, while others ran around and appealed for donations. The spirit of sacrifice is difficult to quantify. The nation, already weakened by exploitation, has suffered such a terrible catastrophe. Although years have passed, the wounds have not yet fully healed. Unless one is forgetful, how can one not feel a sense of trepidation? Now that the peach blossom flood season has arrived again, and disaster is imminent, we, like birds startled by the bow, feel apprehension for the future and dare to use the already moving events to awaken the ears and eyes of the people. We will not refrain from persistent admonishments.

The engineering project to close the breach in the Yellow River has been urged and promoted, and the report from Dongzhuang recently announced the imminent closure of the river. The residents living near the water have been worried for a long time, and this comforting news is better than nothing and is welcomed by everyone. However, the sediment flow of the Yellow River and the volume of the floodwaters have been increasing year by year, while the downstream river channel is narrow and silted up. In addition, the winter freeze was particularly severe, with heavy snow accumulation in the upper reaches. Once the summer season arrives, the melting ice is likely to cause surges. This is something that Mr. Kong Xianrong, who is in charge of closing the breach, has clearly stated. The dangerous and stable situation of the river section changes rapidly, and Mr. Kong also believes that it is not easy to predict. Now, at the beginning of the peach blossom flood season, the water level downstream has been raised repeatedly, and there are urgent reports from the river works in Hebei and Shandong. It is difficult to be optimistic that we can avoid breaches during this year's flood season. As for the Yangtze River, although the people's embankments in various counties have been largely repaired, the overall prevention plan is still being developed. The embankment works in the suburbs of Wuhan are delayed and have not yet been completed, and the remote embankments along the Xiang River are also awaiting supervision and promotion. Recently, two typhoons and rainstorms have attacked Wuhan. Is this not a warning from heaven to the people of Hubei? We silently observe that this year's flood situation is likely to be more severe than before, while most of the water control projects are still stagnant. If the authorities do not strive with increased effort and plan ahead, the fear of the people will be difficult to dispel.

Recently, the Economic Committee has notified the flood prevention bureaus of various provinces to start flood prevention work earlier. Kong Xiangrong has also returned to Jinan to discuss Yellow River management with Han Fuqu. Experts from the League of Nations, such as water conservancy experts Gustav and Ponderley, have been dispatched to Wuhan to inspect the embankment works. The authorities' concern for the people's suffering can be seen from this. We sincerely hope that those in charge will be mindful of past failures, resolutely seek self-improvement, use coordination as a basis, and be realistic as a reliance. Everyone should think of fulfilling their own responsibilities and avoid making excuses and shifting blame. They should plan the allocation of engineering projects in advance to avoid panic when danger arises. The lives of millions of people cannot withstand the endless prayers.

Smuggled Goods Shipped From Tianjin Southward Reach 50,000 Tons Per Month 21

(Xuzhou) According to investigations, smuggled goods such as white sugar, cloth, seaweed, and salt shipped from Tianjin southward via the Tianjin-Peixian Railway reach more than 50,000 tons per month. The Tianjin Customs cannot stop it. The Railway Bureau cannot refuse transport because Japanese merchants pay the freight. Various untaxed goods are sold in Jinan, Xuzhou, Bianliang, Zhengzhou, and Bengbu, causing the value of goods from a certain country in Jiangsu, Anhui, Shandong, and Henan provinces to plummet. (Central News Agency Telegram, 23rd)

Legislative Yuan Scheduled to Complete Drafting Constitutional Clauses Work, Both National Assembly Laws Will Soon Be Completed, Fu Bingchang, Lin Bin, and Others Continue Holding Discussions Yesterday 22

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee's report on the review of the draft constitution submitted to the Legislative Yuan lists 23 points that should be further revised, with one opinion attached. The eight-member committee established by the Legislative Yuan to examine and revise the constitution can complete the drafting of the constitutional clauses and texts by the 28th based on the revision points and opinions issued by the central government. Then, it will be submitted to the plenary session of the Legislative Yuan for review. The 24-member committee can also hold its fourth meeting on the 29th to complete the drafting of the reserved clauses and appendixes regarding the distribution of the number of representatives in the National Assembly Representative Election Law and conclude all its work on drafting the two National Assembly laws. As for the central government's decision that the representatives from the Northeast should be combined with the regional election representatives from the provinces and cities for distribution, the 24-member committee only needs to readjust the originally allocated number of regional election representatives. However, the total number of National Assembly representatives remains at 1,200 and has not been increased as a result. (Central News Agency Telegram, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan has scheduled the promulgation of the draft constitution, the National Assembly Organization Law, and the Representative Election Law for May 5. It has decided to hold review meetings continuously. The five-member drafting committee, including Fu Bingchang and Lin Bin, continued to hold discussions on the 25th, carefully organizing the distribution table of the number of representatives for each region and scheduled review meetings for the original five-member drafting committee and the 24-member drafting committee on the afternoons of the 28th and 29th to organize the clauses in the election law and submit them to the plenary session of the Legislative Yuan for discussion one day in advance. According to Fu Bingchang, the draft constitution and the National Assembly Representative Election Law and Organization Law must be submitted to the plenary session of the Legislative Yuan for discussion within the next week. If the plenary session cannot complete the discussion in one day, it will continue to be held on the second day to review and approve the three draft plans and submit them to the Central Political Committee for transfer to the National Government for promulgation. (Special Dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan has scheduled to urgently review important cases such as the draft constitution, the National Assembly Organization Law, the National Assembly Representative Election Law, and the revised Organization Law of the Executive Yuan. It has now been decided to hold two additional temporary meetings in the next week, in addition to the regular meetings. The convocation period for the temporary meetings will be scheduled for May 1 and 2 to continue holding meetings. (Central News Agency Telegram, 25th)

General Overview of the Twenty-Fifth Year Budget 24

(Nanjing) The national general budget for the twenty-fifth year is currently being compiled by the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics in conjunction with various ministries and departments. Regarding the main tax revenue portion of the income, it has been learned from financial circles that customs duties still rank first, salt taxes second, and consolidated taxes third. However, due to reasons such as reduced imports and rampant smuggling, the customs revenue figures have been reduced compared to the twenty-fourth year. At the same time, the consolidated tax figures have increased compared to the twenty-fourth year due to the prosperity of domestic industry and commerce. However, the increase in consolidated taxes is not enough to offset the decrease in customs duties, resulting in a slight shortfall. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

National Product Inspection Committee Holds Group Research Meeting 25

(Nanjing) The National Product Inspection Committee of the Ministry of Industry held a group research meeting on the morning of the 25th, and a plenary meeting at noon. Wu Dingchang and all committee members and experts attended. First, the experts reported their research opinions on various cases, and it was decided that preparations should be started to recruit and train inspection technicians, and examinations will be conducted in different locations. The detailed recruitment methods will be drafted by the experts and submitted to the meeting. An order instructed the Commodity Inspection Bureau of Shanghai to send personnel to Qimen immediately to plan preliminary inspection methods for Qimen tea. The Shanghai Flour Industry Association, etc., requested that the adulteration of wheat be banned, and the association was instructed to contact the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to discuss technical issues. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Extension of Ship Tax License Deadline for Ice-Bound Vessels 26

(Nanjing) Regarding the case in which the Tianjin-Shanghai Shipping Association requested a two-month extension for the original tonnage tax validity period for ships trapped in ice outside Dagu Port, the Ministry of Transportation consulted the Ministry of Finance for handling. The Ministry of Finance has already instructed the customs authorities to order the Inspectorate General of Customs to investigate and report to the Ministry, and has forwarded the reply to the Ministry of Transportation for review. The content of the reply is as follows: After investigation, the ice-bound vessels at Dagu Port this time were indeed due to an unexpected event and suffered great difficulties. The request to extend the deadline for ship tax licenses should be approved in accordance with the law. However, the length of time that each vessel was trapped varies, and none were trapped for as long as two months. If all ship tax license deadlines are uniformly extended by two months, it would obviously be inappropriate. The relevant customs commissioners have been instructed to notify the trapped vessels to submit accurate evidence to the customs, proving how much each vessel was delayed according to the original schedule, and then extend the license deadline separately according to the number of days delayed, to ensure fairness. However, the methods determined this time are for a special situation and should not be regarded as a regular practice in the future. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Fujian Province Divided into Three Pacification Zones 28

(Fuzhou) Fujian Province's pacification zones are divided into three zones, with Zhang Fang, Liu Heding, and Li Yannian serving as commanders of the first, second, and third zones, respectively. The counties under each pacification zone have been redefined. The first zone governs 20 counties, including Changting, Liancheng, Jianning, Taining, Shaowu, and Jiangle. The second zone governs approximately 23 counties, including Minhou, Luoyuan, Lianjiang, Ningde, Changle, Fuguo, Fuding, Shouning, Xiapu, Gutian, Pingnan, Jian'ou, Jianyang, Nanping, and Pucheng. The third zone governs approximately 20 counties, including Longxi, Jinjiang, Putian, Datian, Yongchun, Minguo, and Yongtai. The establishment of the headquarters of each zone is expected to be in the middle of next month. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Anhui River Dikes Have Been Completely Completed 29

(Wuhu) Except for the two sections of Guangji and Tongren on the Anhui River dike, which are still under construction, the rest have been completed. On the 25th, the river water rose to 17.6 feet, and the Construction Department has issued a notice to all counties to prepare for floods in advance. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Executive Yuan Investigates the Actual Work of Personnel in Various Agencies 30

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan, in view of the fact that the duties of personnel in various subordinate agencies are not clearly defined according to their nature, resulting in mismatches between work and pay, and between positions and responsibilities, and that promotions, demotions, and performance evaluations are also without any reliable standards, has decided to thoroughly understand the actual situation and will begin investigating the working conditions of various ministries, commissions, and administrations next week. The investigation procedures are: first, to formulate a position analysis questionnaire for personnel below the recommended level, and order them to submit it within two weeks; second, to send personnel to various agencies for on-site investigations; and then, based on these two types of information, to combine and refer to them, to statistically analyze the situation of general civil servants from the individual circumstances of personnel, and finally to analyze the work itself and to establish rational positions to build the foundation of career officials in the government. The working conditions of personnel above the recommended level will also be investigated separately at the same time to seek adjustments. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

General Manager of Xindu Bathhouse in Beijing Arrested 31

(Nanjing) Liu Yonglu, the general manager of the Xindu Bathhouse, was arrested by the Capital District Court on the afternoon of the 24th. After being interrogated once, he was released on bail of 3,000 yuan. The case is under investigation. As soon as the investigation is completed, a public prosecution will be filed. Another corpse was dug up in the boiler room of the bathhouse on the morning of the 25th, and digging will continue on the 26th. It is currently difficult to predict whether there are any remaining corpses. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) In order to provide relief to the qualifications of civil servants who have fled from the Northeast, the Ministry of Personnel has decided to extend the re-registration period for personnel who have held positions in the four northeastern provinces to the end of June, but only for those who have submitted cases for review. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

The estimated local income is 4,736,083 yuan, and the estimated local expenditure is 5,575,471 yuan, with a shortfall of 839,388 yuan. The total shortfall for national and local expenditures is 2,377,205 yuan. The reason for this is the decrease in income and the expansion of expenditures. The reason for the insufficient income is entirely due to the impact of the phased prohibition of opium and the abolition of harsh taxes, and the conversion of military colonies into civilian ones. The income has decreased by more than 3.4 million yuan compared to the 23rd year, resulting in a shortfall of 2,377,700 yuan this year. If the income can still maintain the situation in the 23rd year, then not only will the income and expenditure be balanced, but there will also be a surplus of more than 1 million yuan. The Palestine Problem: The Causes and Consequences of the Conflict Between the Arab and Jewish Nations, Leaders of Both Sides Narrate the Story, the British Authorities are in a Dilemma 44

(Jerusalem) After the conflict between Arabs and Jews, Fakri, the Arab Muslim leader and Chairman of the Muslim Committee, recently stated to our interviewer that Arabs and Jews have lived peacefully in Palestine for two centuries and have always maintained good relations. After the British government appointed Storrs as the military governor of Palestine, Storrs organized a Jewish National Home without consulting the people. The Arab and Jewish nations developed resentment because of this. Later, at the end of the European War, during the Versailles Peace Conference, Dr. Weizmann, in the name of the Jewish National Delegation, advocated the restoration of the Jewish state and organized a parliament for it. For the Arabs, they wanted to live and work in peace in their own country, and they should naturally reject foreigners entering their territory in order to maintain their national independence. By 1919, a democratic parliamentary system was established in the Jewish National Home. The Arabs also convened a congress and demanded its cancellation. Subsequent congresses also made such demands, but they were not satisfied, and the disturbances began from that year and have continued to occur. Previously, in 1930, a British parliamentary delegation was sent to Palestine to conduct an investigation. The conclusion was that the land held by each Muslim should be increased from an average of two acres to three acres as a relief measure. This proposal was subsequently passed by the British House of Commons and published in a white paper, becoming the established policy of the British government. However, the Jews immediately opposed it, and Prime Minister MacDonald revoked the white paper two weeks later. Since then, the land owned by Jews in Palestine has been increasing day by day, while the land owned by Muslims has been decreasing day by day. Up to now, Arabs are convinced that the British government is still being oppressed by the Jews in the country. If this continues, all the land owned by Arabs will inevitably be exploited and they will be forced to flee abroad. This is why we are indignant. The Arabs have failed to advocate justice by peaceful means. The British government can only express sympathy for us, otherwise we will not only not support Britain, but will treat it as the greatest enemy. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

(Jerusalem) The Arab Muslim leader Fakri yesterday gave a statement to our interviewer on the past relationship between Jews and Arabs, the causes of the current conflict, and declared that if the British government cannot express sympathy for the Arabs, they will not only not support Britain, but will treat it as the greatest enemy. Joseph, a member of the Jewish People's Assembly, also gave a statement to our interviewer, responding to Fakri's remarks, saying, "There is no fear of not having a place to live for Arabs and Jews who live together in Palestine. It is hoped that the leaders of the Arab nation will deeply understand this point." As far as we Jews are concerned, we will never give up the ideal of building a nation in Palestine, and we have great trust in the British government. Since the immigration of Jews to this area and the increase in the number of people, we also hope that the Arabs will therefore have to seek a compromise with us. In short, we do not intend to change our policy, and we very much hope that the promises previously provided by the British government can also be fulfilled at this time. As for the land issue, the Arabs often say that the Jews have seized and annexed land. In fact, whether they sell their land or not, the right is in their hands, and it has nothing to do with the Jews. Furthermore, the remarks made by the Muslim leader Fakri yesterday threatening the British government are meaningless. "It should be known that after the European War, Britain has allowed the Arab nation to establish several independent kingdoms as a reward for their participation in the war. Therefore, for the sake of the interests of the Arabs, whether they should support Britain, they must know how to plan for themselves." (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Jerusalem) Our interviewer recently visited a British official in the Governorate of Jerusalem and asked about the conflict between Arabs and Jews. The reply was: "We have no grasp on what the future holds, which is truly unfortunate." Our interviewer asked about the severity of the incident, and the official said, "I also have some knowledge of it." Our interviewer then visited Roca, the acting mayor of Tel Aviv, a city where Jews are concentrated, and a member of the Jewish National Committee. He explained in detail the Jewish point of view, stating, "Tel Aviv is vibrant and can be called the best in the world. The 150,000 residents of the city are known for their law-abiding and industriousness, which has led to local prosperity. Jews and Arabs share the benefits. In addition, compulsory education has been implemented in the city, and children can attend school for free, which is unique in the Near East. It can be seen that the Jews' achievements in culture are also very great. It is a pity that although Britain has promised to protect our safety, we are now surrounded on all sides. The atrocities committed by Arabs in various places recently are truly appalling. Jews are often attacked for no reason, and even killed. But we firmly believe that justice still exists, and the world will not fail us. Therefore, we still work as usual, hoping to benefit ourselves and others. However, officials in various places do not punish troublemakers according to the law, which has harmed peace-loving people, which we regret. It is hoped that world consciousness can exert pressure on the authorities in various places in Palestine to curb violence and prevent it from spreading, which would be good." (Havas dispatch, 24th)

(Jerusalem) Our correspondent reports that the situation here today is still peaceful. Since Friday is the day of prayer for Arabs, the leaders of the tribe advised the believers to remain calm beforehand. Therefore, as soon as the prayer ceremonies in various temples were completed, they dispersed peacefully without causing trouble. Demonstrations were held in Haifa, Tulkarm, and Amman, but no major disturbances occurred. Among them, some houses in the Jewish residential area of Haifa were set on fire by Arabs, resulting in considerable losses. According to Jewish sources, the current situation is gradually improving, which is probably a sign of the situation stabilizing. However, the Arabs still claim that they will fight to the end unless their demands are completely satisfied. (Note: The Arabs have two demands: 1. Jews must not buy land in Palestine; 2. Immigration of Jews to Palestine should be stopped by all means.) The leaders of the Arab tribes have also scheduled a meeting for tomorrow to discuss the course of action. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Britain and France Demand Explanation from Germany on Several Points; Submission Planned Soon 45

(London) According to this newspaper's reporter, the French government wishes to understand three things regarding the German memorandum of March 31: Does German leader Hitler view himself solely as the leader of the people of Germany proper, or does he also view himself as the leader of German minorities in Austria, Czechoslovakia, the autonomous region of Memel, and the Free City of Danzig? Does German leader Hitler believe he has already obtained equal rights, or if not, what methods does he plan to use to obtain these rights? Is Germany prepared to participate in mutual assistance organizations? If not, will the issue of whether mutual assistance pacts can be reconciled with non-aggression pacts (as suggested by Germany) be debated again? French Ambassador Corbin raised a private memorandum including these questions during his meeting with British Under-Secretary Sir Robert Vansittart on Wednesday. Furthermore, what is Germany's true intention regarding the issue of ethnic minorities, and does it intend to revise its current borders? This is also something France urgently wants to know. As for whether the list of questions the British government should raise regarding the German memorandum will explicitly address the colonial issue or only allude to it vaguely, it is still unknown at this time. In short, while the questions raised by the French government are generally more practical than those the British intend to raise to Germany, the views of the British and French governments are ultimately in agreement. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(London) In accordance with the resolutions passed at the Second Locarno Conference, the British government will submit a list of questions to Germany, asking it to provide supplementary explanations for the memorandum of March 31. French Ambassador to Britain Corbin met with Under-Secretary of State Vansittart this morning, marking the beginning of these consultations. It is reported that Ambassador Corbin clearly explained to the Under-Secretary the points that France wishes to understand, particularly Germany's attitude towards Austria, Czechoslovakia, and Lithuania, which is of great concern to France. However, it is generally expected that while the note that Britain is to deliver to Germany will be based on France's concerns, it will not list all the points mentioned by France, as the note is usually drafted solely by the Foreign Office and not jointly by Britain and France. Furthermore, it is generally believed that the British note will definitely mention the conclusion of a Western European air pact, stressing that this move is an urgent matter that cannot be ignored. French Chamber of Deputies to Hold Re-election Today; Left Wing Expected to Win 46

(Paris) The re-election of the Chamber of Deputies is scheduled to begin this Sunday (i.e., the 26th). According to general observation, the next Chamber of Deputies will likely be more left-leaning. The Communist Party, which holds twelve seats in the current Chamber, will likely maintain its current position, while the seats held by the Socialist Party and the Radical Socialist Party are certain to increase, although the rate of increase is still unknown. There are a total of 618 seats in the Chamber of Deputies, and the total number of candidates is 4,807. Broadly speaking, they can be divided into three factions: The left-wing Popular Front, which includes: A. Communist Party leader Thorez, B. Orthodox Socialist Party leader Léon Blum, C. Radical Socialist Party leader and former Prime Minister Daladier, D. Republican Socialist Union Party leader and Minister without Portfolio Peng Gu, E. Social Front leader Pétain. The right-wing National Front, which includes a majority of party groups, the most important of which are: A. Republican Democratic Union Party leader and former Minister without Portfolio Marin, B. Central Republican Party leader and former Prime Minister Tardieu, although Tardieu himself has already retired from parliamentary life. The above-mentioned right-wing parties all have politically-oriented groups as their backing, such as the "Patriotic Youth League" and the "Cross of Fire" (organized by right-wing war veterans). The central parties, the most important of which are: A. Democratic Alliance Party leader and Foreign Minister Flandin, B. People's Democratic Party, whose power is limited to certain regions where Catholics congregate. In addition to the above-mentioned left, right, and central factions, there are also several small party groups that occupy a portion of political power solely based on the personal prestige of their members. Moreover, among the three factions above, internal discipline within the left wing is far more strict, while candidates from the right and central factions often attack each other due to personal grievances, which hinders the electoral situation. The current election campaign is extremely intense. Communist Party members, because of the internationalism they have long advocated, have found it difficult to win the approval of the general left-wing, so they have changed their tune and are touting patriotism as a rallying cry. As for the right-wing parties, they often use the controversy caused by the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact and the internal turmoil in Spain after the left-wing victory in the Spanish parliamentary elections as campaign tools. All of these are distinctive features of the election campaign. In addition, in some rural areas, there are still candidates nominated by a majority of agricultural organizations who are advocating plans to protect agriculture and are running for election, but whether they can seize a portion of the seats from the left and right factions is still unknown. According to past practice, candidates who obtain more than half of the votes in the first round of voting (April 26) are elected; otherwise, a second round of voting must be held on May 3, at which time only a relative majority is required to be elected. In general, since the number of candidates listed on the candidate list is so large, the competition will be extremely fierce, so the number of those elected in the first round of voting will not exceed 200. However, the composition of the future Chamber of Deputies should be roughly discernible after the first round of voting. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Lyon: Herriot, former leader of the Radical Socialist Party, delivered a campaign speech last night, defending the financial methods of the party's cabinets over the past four years (Note: The previous Chamber of Deputies was established in May 1932 and completed its term in April 1936, a term of four years), and said that the various cabinets had raised agricultural product prices and the economy was able to recover, the party had made real contribution. Secondly, regarding foreign policy, he said that "France's greatest hope" lies in the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact and the effective alliance treaty between France and Czechoslovakia. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Valence, France: Daladier, leader of the Radical Socialist Party and former Prime Minister, delivered a campaign speech via radio last night, stating briefly: "We French should coexist with all countries and jointly organize a peace mechanism, regardless of the political systems of other countries. The so-called peace mechanism should aim for collective security and arms limitation." He then spoke about the domestic economy, saying that powerful trusts should be attacked, saying that this kind of combination can monopolize finance and hinder small and medium-sized industrial and commercial enterprises, which is actually the political and religious order of the past reappearing in today's economic life. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Deputy Pétain, leader of the left-wing Social Front, recently delivered a campaign speech via radio, stating briefly: "The 38 million people in our country's agricultural, industrial, petty bourgeoisie, and working classes must eliminate their suspicions and unite as one to fight against the despicable and hateful tyrannical system, namely the trusts." Regarding foreign policy, Pétain advocated that France should live peacefully with any country, regardless of its domestic political system, and that peace can be expected by stopping the arms race, establishing a mutual assistance system, and revising existing treaties in accordance with Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant to realize equal rights. Regarding domestic affairs, he said that the Bank of France, colluding with arms dealers, flour merchants, insurance companies, etc., has formed trusts to control politics, which urgently needs to be reorganized to become a public utility. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

(Paris) Colonel de la Rocque, leader of the far-right "Cross of Fire" recently delivered a radio speech, stating briefly: "Now there are those who tout revolutionary doctrines, imitating us, singing the praises of compromise, but in reality, they are partisan and exclusive, and their accumulated mistakes are difficult to reverse. What they advocate is nothing but the aggravation of hatred, and what they claim to be working hard for is nothing but the leading of our country into the abyss of dictatorship. What kind of dictatorship is this? I really cannot bear to say it. Moreover, these people are full of benevolence and morality, but in reality, they are walking hand in hand with the scum and criminals who are hated by the international community to implement a policy of aggression. Why don't you devote your enthusiasm to realizing the beautiful ideals of the 'Cross of Fire'? The dictatorial systems of Fascism, National Socialism, and Bolshevism are all the same in our eyes and are not what we want." (Havas dispatch, 24th)

German Rearmament (Part 1) 47

— Louis Fischer, translated by Bin Fu

The most important question that I hoped to have answered during my stay in Berlin was: would Germany's food and financial panic greatly affect the completion of its military buildup plan? Now I know that the answer is no.

Germany's industrial production has reached a postwar peak. But most of it is neither edible nor wearable. Germany has frozen a large amount of its capital in military supplies. According to experts, there are now three million more people employed than in January 1933—over 750,000 are ordinary employees, over 750,000 are soldiers and sailors, and over 1.5 million are workers; but the amount of goods consumed is still extremely low in proportion. From January 1933 to October 1934, the actual wages of workers and small employees decreased by 25%, and the general decline in the German standard of living under Hitler was about 30% to 35%. If the poor quality of the products is also taken into account, the situation is even worse. Hitler and many newspapers predicted even greater difficulties and sacrifices in 1936. Joseph Winschun said in the Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung on December 31 of last year: "The level of wages can hardly tolerate further price increases." Goebbels said that wages cannot be increased. However, the lack of food is driving up prices. As Winschun himself said, "Exports must be encouraged, and the standard of living should be reduced for this purpose." There are no promises of relief or improvement for 1936. However, discerning observers, both German and foreign, believe that the production of the German military industry will indeed be greatly intensified in the first six months of 1936, and will only slow down after June due to a severe cash crunch. The technical equipment of the German army—airplanes, artillery, tanks, etc.—will reach its peak in 1936, at which time the army will be fully combat-ready.

However, from another perspective, 1936 cannot be said to be the time when Germany's rearmament is complete. National conscription has only just begun, and the ranks of the Reichswehr are not enough to fight a major power. The increased number of officers and staff also lack the effectiveness and knowledge required for modern warfare. The veterans of the European War are old and physically unfit, and their skills are outdated. Germany must wait, waiting for the newly conscripted millions of young people to become soldiers capable of enduring long and arduous wars. But when will this be? Some experts say it will be in 1937, most say it will be in 1938, and some say it will be in 1939. The Reichswehr now has approximately 800,000 officers and soldiers combined, and by 1939, it will have 1 million armed soldiers and 2.5 million reservists, which is enough ammunition and food for a major initial battle.

The main problem is raw materials. The government will try its best to purchase fats from overseas through "clearing agreements," but will also use foreign currency as much as possible to exchange for the import of raw materials. If faced with a blockade or League of Nations sanctions, Germany may not be able to sustain a long-term war due to its limited natural resources. Germany's annual oil consumption is 3.5 million tons, and very little is developed domestically. In many places, although the mines have been dug and oil sprouts have been discovered, the oil wells have been closed, awaiting future development. The synthetic oil manufacturing industry has made astonishing progress. Germany is already able to produce one-third of its annual gasoline consumption, and this could increase to two-thirds in 1938 and 100% in 1939. If private cars on the road disappear, the domestic gasoline production in 1938 will be enough to offset the need for gasoline imports. Germany is now stockpiling large amounts of oil. Friendly countries are helping. The air force needs the highest quality oil, and Germany lacks oil refining technology and experience. Therefore, The American Socony-Vacuum Company recently built a refinery in Hamburg specializing in the refining of aviation oil, which will be completed this year.

Laboratories everywhere are researching substitutes for steel, iron, copper, cotton, and sulfur. The government has scientific records of the industrial uses of all non-ferrous metals. In wartime, these reserves—such as underground telegraph lines—will be used. Germany is also investing in the production of Hungarian soybeans, Yugoslavian bauxite, and Bulgarian tobacco. Of the three million shares in Austria's largest metallurgical plant, Alpine-Montan Company, Germany's Vereinigte Stahlwerke owns 1.7 million shares. Germany is doing this in the hope of obtaining a supply of raw materials from these sources in wartime.

Military orders are the most important food for Germany's heavy industry, and the activities of heavy industry are entirely dominated by military plans. The Opelt car factory in Brandenburg is being built under the supervision of the military. In Germany, there are also ordinary motorcycle factories and the factories of the International Telephone and Telegraph Company, which, although American capital, do not allow any Americans to enter; because they manufacture military equipment.

The whole of Germany is a large military camp. People like me who have been away from Germany for a long time can see the increasing number of Wehrmacht soldiers and uniforms. Now, the ordinary military vehicles speeding through the streets of Berlin are disguised. This is one aspect of actual rearmament. But it is also one aspect of psychological rearmament. Speaking of psychological rearmament, it is now being carried out extremely intensely every day and every hour in newspapers, radio broadcasts, and schools.

Germany's psychological mobilization is very important. Every country is openly expanding its military. This phenomenon has become a norm, and no one thinks about the shoes, socks, shirts, bread, meat, butter, medicine, comfort, and happiness that are stolen from tens of millions of people every day. Sometimes people even conclude that humanity, which is trending towards such a crazy state, should have a war to purify itself. Psychological mobilization is stimulating people to accept the impoverished conformity that results from the expansion of armaments. Every government tells its people that armaments are necessary to protect or maintain national prestige and glory. German newspapers often pay tribute to Hitler because his conscription speech on March 16, 1935, restored Germany's pride and confidence. It is said that Germany has concentrated its industrial strength on rearmament for this reason. I do not underestimate the political significance of nationalism and patriotism. But I do not believe that the main goal of the Nazi's military buildup plan is to satisfy this kind of sentiment. There must be other goals. Is it territorial aggression? German politicians deny it, but what else could it be? They protest and deny it, but in fact, Germany's blaming of Bolshevik Russia for launching an invasion attempt is the same as Rome's blaming of Abyssinia for being the aggressor. Germans insist that they are peaceful, and Hitler's several speeches are often cited by Berlin as proof of Germany's deep love of peace. But can objective truth be sought from those who argue vehemently?

Germans have often been known as inept diplomats, because they do not trust diplomacy much and therefore devote little effort to it. They respect strength; they mock empty talk. One day in 1933, Hitler came to power. Poland was shocked. Because in the previous year, the League of Nations had allowed Germany military equality, Warsaw was terrified that an armed Germany ruled by absolute nationalist Nazis would seriously threaten Danzig and the Corridor. Therefore, in March 1933, the late General Piłsudski concentrated five major army corps near the German border and responded to the Anglo-French attempt to launch a war against Fascist Germany. It is said that the then French Chief of Staff Weygand paid great attention to this idea. By April, Polish troops had occupied the narrow strip of Westerplatte in the Danzig area. It looked like war was about to begin. On May 17, 1933, Hitler delivered a lengthy peace speech in the Reichstag, in which he cleverly declared: "A new European war cannot create a situation better than today. ... Germany is always willing to assume further international security obligations. ... Germany is prepared to abolish all its military facilities." Most countries in the world did not know that this promise was intended to ward off an impending war. The Western European powers were naturally happy to hear Hitler's words, because they did not want to fight. Paris also finally rejected Piłsudski's proposed prevention of war.

Page 8

Second Air Defense Drill in Hangzhou 48

(Hangzhou) The city of Hangzhou held its second air defense drill tonight. The alarm was sounded at 8:00 p.m., and military police and Boy Scouts from various schools were dispatched for guard duty, implementing light and traffic control. Citizens remained quite calm. The air defense department conducted aerial inspections. The alarm was lifted at 9:00 p.m., and the results were quite good. (Special dispatch, 25th)
