Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Imai Denies Signing Anti-Communist Pact, Says Talk of Expanding Japanese Military Presence is Inaccurate, Nagami Also Did Not Discuss North China Diplomacy

(Beiping Correspondence) Imai Takeo, military attaché at the Japanese Embassy in Beiping, has recently established a practice of meeting with Chinese and foreign journalists every Friday. Today (the 24th) was the first such meeting, and many reporters attended, divided into three groups. First, reporters from European and American countries were met, followed by Japanese reporters, and finally Chinese reporters. The following is a record of his remarks:

Mr. Imai began by telling the reporters, "Today's meeting with you has no real news to report. However, I have heard rumors of a general strike and demonstrations by students in Tianjin, which, thanks to the effective prevention by the local Public Security Bureau, did not materialize. As far as I (Imai referring to himself) can tell, this rumored unrest among Tianjin students was not without manipulation. The student movement in Shanghai last year is a clear example. Furthermore, after the recent incursion of communist bandits into Shanxi, the communist party members lurking in Beiping and Tianjin have been very active and are said to have established a branch in Tianjin responsible for command. Therefore, Japan is particularly concerned about the future security of the two cities. The activities of the Communist Party in North China are not only harmful to China but also have a direct impact on Japan. The North China authorities are currently making progress on the path to reconstruction, and their precautions against the current communist threat are considerable. However, they should go further to eliminate hidden dangers in order to achieve political progress. Today, I read an editorial in a Chinese newspaper that referred to the Communist Party as 'new national traitors' and 'new Chinese collaborators.' I wholeheartedly agree and sincerely hope that the Chinese authorities will act accordingly to ensure the tranquility of North China."

At this point, someone asked Imai about the widespread reports in European and American newspapers that China and Japan had signed a joint anti-communist agreement and would expand the Japanese military presence in North China to the Beining, Pinghan, and Pingsui railways. Imai replied, "The above is completely unfounded. Although rumors have been rampant recently, they are all nonsense. The so-called signing of an anti-communist agreement is absolutely untrue. The talk of expanding the area of the Japanese garrison is also absolutely inaccurate. Chief of Staff Nagami recently returned to Japan to attend a division commanders' conference, completed his business, and returned to his post to convey the intentions of the military headquarters. Therefore, I and Major General Matsumuro are preparing to go to Tianjin tomorrow morning to receive a report. Oki, the director of the Zhangjiakou Special Agency, has also been summoned to Tianjin. We will not stay long in Tianjin because the 27th is the day of the memorial service for the war dead, so we must rush back to Beiping before then to preside over the ceremony. As far as I know, Chief of Staff Nagami has not met with the responsible Chinese authorities as of the 22nd. In short, if there is a need for Chinese and Japanese officials and civilians to discuss anti-communism, there is no need for secrecy, and outsiders should not speculate, which only leads to confusion."

Imai continued to discuss the situation of suppressing bandits in Shanxi, saying, "Initially, the situation was very critical, but now it has eased. It is like a patient who was initially in a critical acute condition and has now turned to a chronic one. Recovery will take time, which is to be expected. As for diplomatic negotiations, I have heard nothing so far. The issue of building the Cangshi Road is only mentioned in the newspapers. This may have been a proposal made by the Chinese railway authorities during their inspection in the north some time ago. Now the newspapers are reporting that this matter has been concretized, but I am very skeptical of this statement and cannot believe it. Consul General Kawagoe Mao of Tianjin will be promoted to Chinese ambassador. Kawagoe himself had no prior knowledge of this. I do not know when he will return to Japan for instructions." Finally, when asked about the drug prohibition issue, he said, "I have heard that the efforts to prohibit drugs in various counties of eastern Hebei have been quite successful with the assistance of the Japanese military authorities, and there is a possibility of eliminating them completely. However, the number of opium dens opened by Koreans in Beiping and Tianjin has recently expanded. What are your opinions as a military attaché?" Imai pondered for a moment and replied, "I strongly support the suppression of potent drugs. It is very gratifying that the drug atmosphere in various counties of eastern Hebei is gradually being eliminated. It is necessary to suppress opium dens in Beiping and Tianjin. However, in my opinion, it is necessary to prohibit both selling and buying. I hope that China and Japan will cooperate to achieve success. The policy of prohibiting buying depends on education and law working together." At this point, the reporters took their leave. (24th)

Chiang Kai-shek's Speech: The Bright Path for the People of Sichuan (Continued) At the Expanded Memorial Week of the Sichuan Provincial Party Headquarters

First, "Loyalty and courage are the foundation of patriotism," which means that the moral qualities of loyalty and bravery are the fundamental requirements for our patriotism. To love and save our country, we must first cultivate the spirit and virtues of loyalty and courage. At the same time, our loyalty and courage must be used to love and save the country and our compatriots, and must be for the public and not for the private, for others and not for oneself. For example, the courage of ordinary bandits who kill and rob, and of those who fear death and are unwilling to face danger, is also a kind of courage. However, this kind of courage is entirely for personal gain and therefore becomes a crime and cannot be considered loyalty and courage. Therefore, the true meaning of loyalty and courage is what the ancients called "devotion to the country," "sacrificing oneself for righteousness," "forgetting oneself for the public, forgetting one's family for the country," and "being brave in public battles and timid in private fights."

Second, "Filial piety is the foundation of managing a family," which means that if we want to make our family harmonious, orderly, and consistent, and create a peaceful and happy family, we must start with being filial to our parents. Because we must fulfill our filial duties, then there will be a distinction between superiors and inferiors, and an order between elders and juniors, so that the affairs of the family can be managed in an orderly manner. Reason can be promoted and magnified.

Third, "Benevolence is the foundation of dealing with things." The so-called "dealing with things" includes interpersonal relations and the handling of affairs. Our standard for dealing with things is "benevolence," which is what the ancients called "benevolence to the people and love for all things." We must love our compatriots, love our friends, and even love humanity and all things in the universe. The so-called "people are our compatriots, and things are our partners," "heaven and earth coexist with us, and all things are one with us," is the spirit of benevolence. If we treat people, deal with affairs, and use things with this great spirit, we will surely be loved by people everywhere, get help from people, and exhaust the resources of things. In this way, one point of our own efforts can produce at least ten points of effect. All the power we receive can become our power and can increase countless times.

Fourth, "Trustworthiness is the foundation of establishing a career." If we want to make a career, we must gain people's trust and help. To gain people's trust and help, we must first have trustworthiness ourselves. In dealing with people, we must first show our faith and morality in practice, so that people will believe us and know that we are not people who are unfaithful, unrighteous, selfish, or afraid of death. We must first have a sense of righteousness and faith, and then people will trust us, and then we can succeed in our careers.

Fifth, "Peace is the foundation of dealing with the world." The so-called "peace" refers to the relationship between people. "Harmony" means loving each other and not having jealousy, suspicion, cursing, fighting, or even fratricide. "Peace" means being fair to each other and not having encroachment, contention, bullying, partiality, or harming others for one's own benefit. There must be fairness in order to have love, and there must be peace in order to deal with the world. Individuals in society must treat others with peace. All our compatriots must love each other. We must be willing to suffer losses ourselves and not take advantage of others. We must know that those who advocate justice and maintain peace will surely achieve ultimate success. Those who suffer small losses in the present will surely gain advantages in the end. Those who take small advantages in the present will surely suffer great losses in the end. All our compatriots must understand this principle and live together in peace. Our first step is to realize the eternal peace of the entire country and create the most peaceful country. The second step is to contribute our Chinese peace to the world and realize universal peace throughout the world. Peace is an inherent virtue of our China. We always advocate peace. However, in order to maintain the survival of the country and the survival of the nation, we must have the ability and determination to defend ourselves. If foreigners want to invade us and oppress us, they are destroying peace and disturbing peace. In order to maintain justice and righteousness, we have no choice but to resist in order to strive for lasting peace. Therefore, when all peaceful means have been exhausted and peace is no longer possible, we can only and must seek independent existence and consolidate peace through means other than peaceful means.

Sixth, "Etiquette is the foundation of managing affairs." This means that if we want to do things well, we must pay attention to etiquette. Because without etiquette, there will be no order in society or in human affairs, and there will be no stability. The relationship between people will be even more chaotic, and nothing can be done. For example, there are more than a thousand people present today. If there is no etiquette, how can we move and act in unison and in an orderly manner? Not to mention the discipline of a large number of people and groups, even individual life and work are the same. The ancients said, "Etiquette is reason," which means that when we live and do things, we must have order, restraint, and proper and reasonable attitudes and rules. When we live and do things, we must pay attention to etiquette at all times, otherwise we cannot be human beings, let alone do things. Therefore, it is said that "without etiquette, there is no way to stand," "etiquette is the management of affairs - gentlemen have their affairs, and they must have their management - without etiquette, there is no place for hands and feet, no place for eyes and ears, no control over advancing and retreating, and no strategy for hunting and military affairs, and no system for military and martial arts." The so-called "etiquette is the foundation of governing the world" in this code of conduct means the same thing.

Seventh, "Obedience is the foundation of responsibility." If we want to make the country rich and strong, the people must be able to assume responsibility and work together. How can this responsibility be fulfilled? How can everyone's work be done with twice the result with half the effort? The most important thing is that, in terms of horizontal relations, we must divide labor and cooperate with each other. In terms of vertical relations, we must have layer-by-layer control and level-by-level obedience. For example, the organization of the government has the central government, the provincial government, the county government, and even the district office. The personnel of the various levels of the army have the commander-in-chief, the commander, the division commander, and even the soldiers at all levels. They must all be controlled from top to bottom and obey level by level from bottom to top. Lower-level agencies or personnel must obey the orders of higher-level agencies or officials in order to do things well and fulfill their responsibilities. The reason why we cannot do everything well in our country and the country has been brought to such a critical state of survival is because people only know how to fight for power and profit, and cannot be responsible and fulfill their duties. Everyone wants to talk about freedom and equality, and does not know the principles of obedience and responsibility. They do not know that if everyone talks about freedom and equality casually, the country and the nation will perish. They do not know that modern citizens should sacrifice their own freedom and equality in order to seek the freedom and equality of the entire country. In the future, if we want to save the country, everyone must be responsible. The fundamental prerequisite for responsibility is that everyone must sacrifice their own freedom and equality, obey the government, obey the law, and obey their superiors in order to fulfill their responsibilities. The government is the organ of the country, the law is the will of the country, and the superior is the representative of the government. Therefore, when we obey our superiors, we are not obeying individuals, but obeying the orders they issue in accordance with national laws. In short, our obedience is obedience to the country, is obedience to our duties, and is obedience to our own responsibilities. Because the country is my own, and the job is also my own. Such obedience is also obedience to myself. If I can obey myself, this is called self-discipline. Anyone who can be self-disciplined will succeed. Therefore, we obey for the country, not for any one person, let alone for private individuals. Therefore, this kind of obedience is glorious, not shameful. Only in this way can we be truly obedient, truly responsible, and worthy of being a modern citizen.

Eighth, "Diligence and thrift are the foundation of service." Heaven and earth and parents gave birth to us, and society and the country educated us to become a person. We must serve society and the country. We ourselves are a part of society and the country, so serving society and the country is serving ourselves. I am for everyone, that is, everyone is for me. This is the first priority of self-help and helping others. Only in this way can life have meaning and value. Where should we start serving society and the country? We must be diligent and thrifty. We must be diligent in order to make contributions, and we must be thrifty in order to have restraint and avoid consumption. In the first aspect, the purpose of our diligence and thrift must be to serve the people. Therefore, if diligence and thrift are for private gain and not for public gain, like those who "get up at the crowing of the rooster and work diligently for profit," this kind of diligence and thrift is of no benefit to the country and the people, and is not true diligence and thrift. We must know that living in modern times, without the entire society, the entire nation, and the entire country, there is no way for one person to be warm if everyone is hungry and cold, and for one person to be happy if everyone is in distress. Therefore, we must establish the ambition of "worrying before others and enjoying after others," and develop the spirit of labor and service. To establish others is to establish ourselves, and to save others is to save ourselves.

Ninth, "Cleanliness is the foundation of self-cultivation." The so-called "self-cultivation" refers to the cultivation of both the inner mind and the body. If we want to cultivate ourselves, we must start with cleanliness. We must be inwardly focused, pure, and clear-minded, and outwardly neat, solemn, clean, and bright. Extending this to the things around us and the environment in which we live, we must make them so. Then we can have a strong body, a noble character, and a brilliant mind. Most people do not know the importance of cleanliness. Even like the famous scholars of the past, they claimed to be unkempt and casual, and falsely called it elegance. We should eliminate and wash away this bad habit and shame. But the cleanliness I am talking about is simple and unadorned, and is absolutely different from luxury and splendor. It is not to ask everyone to wear fine silk of different colors, let alone to ask everyone to use foreign goods. This is luxury, and luxury will lead to the destruction of the country and the decline of the nation. Therefore, cleanliness is close to thrift and simplicity, while luxury is completely opposite. This is an additional point of meaning." (To be continued)

Trial of Tan Zhuohong Case: Witnesses Still Need to be Summoned for Further Interrogation

The case of Tan Zhuohong, a judge of the Shanghai Local Court, and Yang Shaopeng, a lawyer, who were secretly accused to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, was previously investigated by the Procuratorate of the Wuxian Local Court, which prosecuted them for dereliction of duty. The trial was held on the 25th. Lawyers Tan Yanwu, Chao Limian, and Yang Yanlu Dingkui defended them. On the witness side, Sun Zuji, Zhu Yisheng, Gao Junxiang, and Li Shirui (deceased) were summoned. Only Zhu Yisheng and Gao Junxiang appeared in court. The trial began at 2:50 p.m. in the third courtroom, with Judge Yu Zhong presiding. Prosecutor Zhu Shufen also attended to perform his duties. After Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng were briefly interrogated, Prosecutor Zhu Shufen stood up and stated the intent of the prosecution. Judge Yu said that the court term for this case was very near, and the summoned witnesses had not arrived in full. He would first interrogate those who had reported. The witness was first interrogated:

Zhu Yisheng testified:

35 years old, from Shanghai, a Chan master. He performed his duties in 1933. He did not know Yang Shaopeng, and he did not have a clear memory of the year before last. He did not know Tan Zhuohong. The official discussed the witness's status with Prosecutor Zhu and ordered him to sign a statement. Zhu also testified that in the case of Qin Zhengru, the owner of the Haizhou ship, who was accused of causing death by negligence, a waiter from the Datong Company found Wu Zhikuan, the ship's mate, and said that if money was not paid, the case would be sentenced to three years in prison. This was what Qin Zhengru told me, indicating that a decision had not yet been made. I did not pay attention to him. In the case of Lei Yunsheng suing Wang Bingnan for counterfeiting trademarks, I was the agent of civil litigation. The case was tried by Tan Zhuohong. Wang Bingnan was released on bail in the first hearing. Later, Yang Shaopeng came to my office and said that Tan Zhuohong told you not to worry about the Qin Zhengru case, saying that things were bad because of someone named Gong. Now, in the Lei Yunsheng case, Tan Zhuohong said that if you paid some money, you could get a satisfactory result. I immediately rejected him and did not ask him what his relationship was with Tan Zhuohong. Later, Yang called again and said that 1,000 yuan would be enough, but I refused again. The first time they asked for 2,000 yuan. Because I did not believe that the court would do such a thing, I did not ask much. At the end of the debate, he called again and said that he would give me one last chance and that at least 400 yuan would be enough. I did not agree. I had talked about this with Lei Yunsheng in some detail. I do not know anyone named Gong. I have no ill intentions towards Tan and Yang.

Gao Junxiang testified:

36 years old, from Jinshan, lives in Shanghai, a lawyer. He knew Yang Shaopeng from childhood, but they did not associate with each other, and he had no bad feelings towards him. In the case of Wu Peizhen suing Li Keting, I was the defense lawyer. As a result, the criminal court did not accept the case. At first, it was handled by Judge Tan Zhuohong, but I don't know who handled it later. I appeared in court once for the second hearing. In ten days, the defendant posted a bail of 1,000 yuan. I immediately asked to replace it with a shop guarantee, but because it was late that day, I did not have time to find a guarantor. The next day, I found a guarantor, but Judge Tan suddenly summoned the guarantor. Later, the family called me and said that Judge Tan told the guarantor that he had to assume a responsibility of 10,000 yuan, so the guarantor refused to guarantee. I was very surprised, so I went to the court to ask Judge Tan what was going on. Judge Tan said, "I'll tell you tomorrow." At that time, the family went to hire Lawyer Lu to handle the case. The next day, Yang Shaopeng came and asked if I had any opinions on this case. I said no. At that time, Lawyer Lu arrived and said that the case should not have been accepted at all, and the detention was ridiculous. Yang Shaopeng listened and said nothing, and then left. At that time, Yang did not call Judge Tan, but I heard Yang say that he was going to talk to Judge Tan. There was nothing else to say.

Yang Shaopeng testified:

I was introduced to Tan Zhuohong by Chen Hanshi and Chen Zongfu last spring in Shanghai. Tan admired Zhang Shizhao's morality and writing and asked Chen Hanshi to introduce him to Zhang's door. Zhang agreed to introduce a friend, and we had dinner at Zhang's house. There were four of us. In the case of Zhang Qidong et al. suing Song Dawei for defamation, I remember that Sun Zuji, a teacher, came to invite me. After I went, he called the waiter and then asked me if I knew Tan Zhuohong. I asked him what he meant. He said, "If you don't know him, then forget it." He looked unhappy. I took my leave. I didn't say that I wanted to think of a way to get the defendant to pay a considerable price for this case. I haven't known Zhu Yisheng for long. Last summer, I met him at the court for a railway case. I went to his office. I don't remember the date. He invited me and told me that he was handling a case of Lei Yunsheng suing Wang Bingnan for counterfeiting trademarks and wanted to ask me to find a way for Judge Tan to order the defendant to pay 30,000 yuan in compensation. I didn't agree, so he resented me. He made false accusations because his coercion failed. I am a classmate of Gao Junxiang. In the Wu Peizhen case, Lawyer Lu said that spouses could not sue each other, so I called Zhang Shizhao to ask for Tan Zhuohong's phone number. I called Tan and told him to handle the case carefully and not to be sloppy and to refer to the law. I wrote a letter to Lawyer Gao, asking him to speak with conscience. In the Li Zhizhi case, I wrote the petition for three days. If I could plead with the court, why would I have worked so hard to write the petition?

Tan Zhuohong testified:

The case of Zhang Qidong suing Song Dawei for defamation was handled by me. The defendant, Ning Dawei, was wanted because his whereabouts were unknown. I had been in Shanghai for a short time. I probably met Yang Shaopeng once at Zhang Shizhao's house. I didn't ask Yang Shaopeng to meet Zhang Shizhao. Chen Zhongfu's house had also been visited. There were no other friends. I knew Zhang Shizhao in Beijing in 1916. I didn't ask Yang Shaopeng to pay Zhang Shizhao as my leader. I didn't ask Yang Shaopeng to say that I wanted money in the Zhang Qidong case. The case of Qin Zhengru of the Haizhou ship was also handled by me. He was sentenced to three years in prison. I forgot how the High Court ruled on the appeal. The Lei Yunsheng case was handled by me. I forgot how Wang Bingnan was sentenced for counterfeiting trademarks. I didn't ask Yang Shaopeng to ask Qin Zhengru for money, and I didn't ask Yang to talk to Lei Yunsheng in the Wang Bingnan case about finding a solution. After the debate, I reopened the debate because the prosecution added another defendant. I went to the Public Security Bureau to investigate. Because the case was important, I reopened the debate, not to leave a chance to get money, but to reopen the debate.

Ma Qinan Road Second Special District Prison warden Jia Furong and warden Ren Wu, formerly assigned to the inmate ward (i.e., Guangci Hospital) to perform their duties, were accused of covering up for and instigating convicted murderer Gu Zhuxuan to smoke opium inside. Hongzhang Cotton Mill Doctor Jin Jianming Arrested; Questioning Girlfriend Led to Gun Threat; Detained and Sent to Court; Hearing Postponed for Further Investigation 54

Jin Jianming, a doctor from Jiangsu working at the Hongzhang Cotton Mill on Maigen Road, was suddenly arrested by detectives from the Yulin Road Police Department on the afternoon before yesterday. A handgun and 21 bullets were found. He was detained in the police department. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Fifth Criminal Court of the First Special District. The Public Works Department lawyer Jiang Baolian filed charges of obstructing freedom under Article 305 of the criminal law, stating that the police department acted on a report from Chen Peiming, the principal of Huacheng School at 42 Lane 376, Dalianwan Road, that the defendant Jin Jianming, along with Liu Zhidong, had visited the school to inquire about Ma Channing, asking about the whereabouts of Wang Shaohan and his wife Liu Xiulan. According to Ma, Wang and his wife had been arrested by the Public Security Bureau on suspicion of being communists but were released on bail and had returned to Luoyang, Henan. However, the defendant did not believe this and insisted on taking Ma Channing to 30 Shude Lane, Dalianwan Road, Wang and his wife's former residence. When they arrived and found that Wang had indeed left, the defendant suddenly became angry, took out a handgun from his suit pocket, loaded it, pointed it at Ma Channing, and demanded the truth. While they were arguing, the landlord Bai Jinwen intervened and persuaded him to put away the gun. The defendant then forced Ma to take a car to the Jing'an Temple Road post office and forced Ma to send a telegram to Luoyang, urging Wang and his wife to return to Shanghai quickly. Ma had no choice but to comply and was then released. The day before yesterday, Ma received several phone calls from the defendant, urging Ma to go to Luoyang to find Liu Xiulan. Ma agreed and told the defendant to come to the school to discuss it yesterday. Ma then reported it to the police department. However, Ma suddenly received a telegram from Wang and his wife in Luoyang, stating their reasons for not being able to come to Shanghai, so when the defendant went to Huacheng School yesterday, he was arrested by detectives. According to the defendant's statement to the police department, he knew Liu Xiulan well and had a deep friendship with her. He had not seen her for over a year. Because Ma Channing was related to Liu, he went to inquire about her. He also led the detectives to the doctor's office in the Hongzhang Cotton Mill and found the gun and ammunition. The case is still under investigation because the accomplices have not been apprehended, and the gun and ammunition have not been examined. The defendant requested a postponement. The defendant Jin Jianming hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him in court. Judge Yang ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody pending further investigation at a later date.

Party and Government Agencies Confer on Establishing Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association; Special District Rickshaw Pullers' Association Petitions Party and Government; Public Works Department to Hold Meeting with Rickshaw Merchants on Pending Issues This Month 55

The Special District Rickshaw Pullers' Association petitioned the Party and government agencies yesterday and sent a letter to rickshaw merchants requesting that mutual aid fees for this month be deposited in a bank. Party and government agencies conferred yesterday on the organization of the Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association. The Public Works Department is scheduled to meet with rickshaw merchants on the 30th of this month to resolve all pending issues. Details are as follows:

Rickshaw Pullers' Petition

The Special District Rickshaw Pullers' Association of this city, to request that Party and government agencies thoroughly investigate the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Association and prepare to initiate the Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association, sent Zhou Weigao, Xia Huaixian, Ma Taizhi, Lu Deguang, Dai Rugui, Yang Xingyou, and others, nine people in total, to petition the City Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday afternoon at 3 PM. Zhu Yangwu represented the City Party Headquarters in receiving them, and Wang Gang, the director of the Labor Welfare Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, received them. After clarifying the points of the petition, they expressed their acceptance and promised to take action and study the matter. Regarding the organization of the Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association, it was decided to implement it in the near future. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Establishing Welfare Association

The Rickshaw Pullers' Association requested Party and government agencies to organize a Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association to handle welfare matters for rickshaw pullers, which has been approved by the authorities. Zhu Yangwu, the clerk of the Civil Affairs Section of the City Party Headquarters, and Wang Gang, the director of the Labor Welfare Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, convened a meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the organization of the Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association, aiming to establish it in the shortest possible time.

Official-Merchant Meeting

According to news from the Public Works Department yesterday, the rickshaw dispute in the Public Concession had previously come to a temporary end. However, to resolve all pending issues, the authorities of the Public Works Department found it necessary to continue negotiations with rickshaw merchants. These negotiations have recently been scheduled for Thursday, April 30, at 9:45 AM at the Public Works Department. Regarding the selection of attendees for the meeting from the rickshaw merchants, the Rickshaw Association held a joint meeting last night and officially determined their representatives, who will base their negotiations on the resolutions of the general membership meeting.

Requesting Return of Association Fees

Rickshaw lessors Shao Zhencai, Qin Jianzhou, Fu Huanzhang, Yuan Guilin, Zhu Deyao, etc., jointly sent a letter to the Rickshaw Association, stating that in order to correct errors, they had, in March, followed the central government's orders and the principles and organizational law of the Rickshaw Pullers' Welfare Association drafted by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and requested guidance from Party and government agencies. To resolve the dispute as soon as possible, the association continued to collect mutual aid fees for April on behalf of the members. As the Public Works Department seemed not to be coercing donations as in the past, it should deposit the fees in a bank for safekeeping or return them to the rickshaw pullers and not hand them over without authorization, pending disposition by the Party and government. Rickshaw puller representatives Xia Huaixiang, Zhou Weigao, etc., also requested the return of this month's mutual aid fees, saying that the rickshaw puller directors violated the wishes of the public and withdrew from the association, so their words and deeds should not be considered representative.

Xue Tingfang Delivers Threatening Letter; Demands Extortion of 500 Yuan; Telephone Negotiation Betrays Accent; Detectives Wait and Arrest Him 57

Chen Yanling, the director of the Commercial Press at 200 Guizhou Road, a native of Shaoxing, received a threatening letter from a gang on the 22nd of this month, intending to extort 500 yuan, and arranged to pay the money at 8 PM that night in a room opened by Dong Cheng at the Dahua Hotel on French Avenue, or else his son would be dealt with using a gun. Chen sent someone to the agreed location, but they returned without meeting anyone. On the morning of the 23rd, Chen received another letter, again arranging to pay the money at the original location that night. Chen reported this to the Lao Zha Police Department, which ordered detectives to wait at the Dahua Hotel, but again, there were no results. At 1:30 PM on the afternoon before yesterday, Chen suddenly received a phone call from someone claiming to be Dong Cheng, discussing the payment, saying that the money had to be picked up at 8 PM that night, but Chen recognized the accent as that of Xue Tingfang, a Shaoxing native who often did business with the bookstore. To confirm this, he asked his colleague Dong Chengde to listen, and Dong also confirmed that it was Xue's accent without a doubt. Chen immediately reported this to the police department, and Detective Chief Zhang Yuanjing and detectives Feng Xiushan, Sun Dafa, and Zhang Yi went to wait around the bookstore. At 7:10 PM, Xue Tingfang indeed arrived, offering to sell two boxes of carbon paper to Chen, and Chen was just about to hand over the money to test his intentions when the detectives stepped forward and arrested Xue, taking him back to the police department. Xue was found to live at 4 Longzhi Lane, Kang Nai Road, and worked as a clerk at the Yizhong Tobacco Company, earning 53 yuan a month. He had previously sold carbon paper to the plaintiff's shop. At first, Xue completely denied threatening Chen Yanling. The detectives then separated the plaintiff and Xue into the Bao Detective Room and the Questioning Room. The Bao Detective Room called the Questioning Room and ordered Xue to talk to Chen. Chen confirmed that the accent on the phone at 1:30 PM that afternoon was the same as Xue's. Xue then admitted that he had ordered a letter-writing stall to write the threatening letter. He was sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District yesterday morning. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the circumstances and filed charges under Article 346, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, also stating that because of the rain yesterday, the letter-writing stall could not be found, so he requested permission to postpone the hearing. Chen Yanling then testified about receiving the letter and phone call. The defendant Xue Tingfang then completely denied everything. Judge Feng Shide examined the evidence and ordered the case to be postponed for further questioning.

American Botanist Mr. Lu Speaks on Strange Sights of Antarctic Exploration; Coldest Climate Reaches 72 Degrees Below Zero; Greatest Reward is the Grand Beauty of Natural Forces 58

The Continental News reports that Mr. Lewis Sorsen, a renowned American botanist and member of the Byrd Antarctic Expedition, recently arrived in Shanghai with his wife and will stay for a few days before touring the Yangtze River and then lingering in North China for several weeks, eventually circumnavigating the globe. Yesterday, Mr. Lu briefly discussed his experiences in Antarctic exploration with guests. He said that the entire team consisted of 55 people and stayed in the "White Hell" for about twenty months. He and Mr. Rupert set off for Little America on October 13, 1933. The team first went to New Zealand and then reached the east side of Little America in December for several aerial reconnaissance missions inland. In early January 1934, they reached the Little America base and set up tents. The shelters built during the previous expedition were still in good condition but needed some repairs. The supply ship "Walker Run Bear" unloaded the necessary supplies and sailed back to Wellington. The team then prepared for a long march. As a botanist in the team, he and several others studied extremely small shrimp-like creatures and mosses that lived in the salty water of the region. He remained with the team until it returned to New Zealand on its way back to America. The journey was fraught with difficulties, as detailed in the book by Byrd and others, so I will not repeat them. Living in the Antarctic during the "Long Night" is unbearable unless one completely changes one's lifestyle. The loneliness of being holed up all day is unbearable for the living. Fortunately, there are many things to do. Sometimes, we work in shifts day and night. The team members engaged in technical affairs are especially busy, and the managers who send moneyless telegrams every night have no spare time. One person is responsible for editing news and writing weekly broadcast messages. For me personally, the greatest reward for staying there is the magnificent beauty of the natural forces around us. For two weeks each month, we live in darkness, seeing only moonlight. This scenery is deeply impressive. The moonlight is almost as bright as sunlight, without the dazzling glare. The light can illuminate miles. The coldest climate the team encountered was in August and September. One day, the thermometer dropped to 72 degrees below zero. At this time, the team members could not hear their own breathing. The breath froze almost immediately upon touching the face. The cold wind was especially fearsome, and fighting against it was extremely difficult. The moonlight and scenery are a sufficient reward for the loneliness, and the "Antarctic Lights" are especially lovely. They can often be seen on clear nights. Their beauty is indescribable.

Recent News from Lun Chang Textile Money Flower Company; Laundry Picture as a Mark, Never Fading; Three-Yard Cheongsam Material Sells for Only One Yuan 64

Lun Chang Textile Dyeing and Printing Company, founded in Shanghai ten years ago, started when China's printing industry was still in its infancy. The company was the first to adopt the latest machinery and set up a factory near the Dalae Wharf in Pudong to undertake printing business. Because of its excellent products, it was extremely popular in all sectors, and its business grew day by day. In 1934, the company, in response to social needs, invested heavily in establishing a large-scale textile factory in Pudong to produce its own cloth. From raw cotton to printing, the company did everything itself, from spinning and weaving to dyeing and printing, without relying on outside sources. At present, the factory employs thousands of workers, who work day and night, and the demand is still greater than the supply. Furthermore, the company, seeing that various printed fabrics sold on the market faded easily and lost the trust of the general public, specially launched a variety of laundry-picture-printed fabrics. These fabrics have bright colors and will not fade for a long time. Even after being exposed to the sun and washed in water, the company guarantees that they will never fade. A small laundry picture guarantee label is affixed to the edge of each piece of fabric every two yards apart for identification. If the color is found to fade within four months of purchase, the faded fabric can be returned to the company for a free exchange, ensuring customer satisfaction. The company also specially manufactures a variety of inexpensive, high-quality, never-fading printed fabrics. These products are durable, brightly colored, and beautifully designed, making them ideal for making summer clothes for women and children. It is said that a three-yard cheongsam material costs only about one yuan in national currency. This price is unprecedented in Shanghai. Yong'an, Sincere, Xinxin, Lihua, Luo, Ailianhui Trading Company, and major cotton shops in this city and other places all sell these products.

Jiangsu Bank to Provide Small Loans; Implemented in Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Xuzhou 71

The Jiangsu Bank is launching small-scale industrial and commercial loans to assist industries in Jiangsu Province. The bank has conducted thorough research beforehand and has completed preparations. The scheme has been implemented in various locations, including Shanghai, Zhenjiang, and Xuzhou. The loan application process is conducted jointly with local chambers of commerce and trade associations. Industrial and commercial enterprises applying for loans are required to provide guarantees from their respective trade associations, which in turn provide guarantees to the chambers of commerce. The chambers of commerce then provide guarantees to the bank. The interest rate is approximately 1%. The loan regulations are currently under review by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance. Once approved, the bank will expand the loan program to other areas.

Renowned Lawyer Zhu Fengchi Passes Away 75

Lawyer Zhu Fengchi, a native of Wuyuan, Huizhou, graduated from the Zhejiang Provincial Law and Politics College. He has been practicing law for more than ten years and is known for his eloquence, responsiveness, and quick understanding. In the early Republic of China, he served as the chief prosecutor of the Jiangsu Wuxi Local Prosecutor's Office but, being indifferent to officialdom, returned to Hangzhou to practice law. He also served as the president of the Zhejiang Prison School and the president of the Zhejiang Commercial Bank. In 1926, he moved his family to Shanghai and did much to help his fellow Wuyuan natives in Shanghai. He was elected chairman of the Wuyuan Shanghai Fellow Association and was elected to the executive committee of the Shanghai Lawyers Association last year. Due to his busy work, he suffered from hemoptysis. After treatment, it improved, but it recurred this spring, complicated by a cold. Medical treatment was ineffective, and he passed away on the 4th of this month. The funeral was held on the 8th at the Haig Road Chinese Funeral Home, with hundreds of relatives and friends attending the funeral ceremony. It is now reported that the memorial service will be held on May 3 at the Chinese Funeral Home, and the coffin will be transported to Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou for burial the next day.

Children's Supplement of Shen Bao, Reading Living Books, Xie Yun. Little friends! Now the spring sunshine is bright, and it is time for your happy travels. You go from the "narrow cage" of school to the school of nature. The myriad of phenomena will overwhelm you. This is the nature school of reading living books. What is a living book? Life! Little friends, do not forget to educate yourselves, and always seek knowledge from your lives. Schools and books, teachers, are just helpers to guide you. In the end, you still need to work hard yourself to gain true knowledge. Everything under the sky and on the earth is a book. Whether you see a plant or an animal, you must observe it carefully and study it earnestly. You can gain all kinds of useful knowledge. Your eyes should always be observing, and your minds should always be thinking! Why could Watt invent the steam engine by paying attention to the lid of a boiling kettle? Why could Newton invent the law of universal gravitation by paying attention to the falling apple? They were both able to read living books, and thus invent such useful new things. Little friends, you must absolutely not only read books with black words on white paper, you must also read living books in order to gain truly useful knowledge, so that you can invent new things like Watt and Newton.

Hiding the Beard in the Sleeve, Schoolteacher. In autocratic times, once a person became a high official, they would put on airs, and every action had to be pretentious and domineering, losing all the free and easy fun. But first-rate, capable people would never be willing to abandon their original nature. So, in their spare time, they would privately travel in disguise to investigate the real situation of society, so as not to be deceived by their subordinates.

When Zeng Guoquan was the Governor-General of Liangjiang, he was already over sixty years old. He often dressed up as a countryman and went around playing. Once, he told his staff member to wear ordinary cloth clothes; he himself wore a felt hat and a short jacket with wide sleeves. In the middle of the night, they went out of Nanjing city, climbed Lion Mountain, and went all the way to the military camp in Xiaguan to take a look. The soldiers and generals in the camp were all asleep. They went to the kitchen and ate some melons and fruits to quench their thirst. Then they went to the pier to enjoy the moon.

It happened that a steamship was coming upstream, and the two of them pretended to be ordinary passengers and took the ship to Hankou. They stayed in a small inn for two days, and then crossed the river to Wuchang. It happened that Zhang Zhidong, the Governor-General of Huguang, was holding a military parade. The generals ascended the platform, looking very majestic. Zeng Guoquan also mingled in the crowd and watched from the side. Because his beard was very long, he held one hand up to his chin and tucked his beard into his sleeve, so as not to be recognized. After having a great time, he quietly returned to Nanjing.

Just imagine, what a calm, alert, and humorous high official he was!

Float and Sink, Zhen.

On Sunday, Min'er was studying alone. He first reviewed nature and read the lesson on submarines. In addition to what the book told him, he had even more questions outside the book. As soon as he had a question, he couldn't figure it out himself, so he went to ask his father and brother, not hiding anything in his mind, and only stopped when he asked clearly. Therefore, his knowledge progressed very quickly, and his father and brother were also very willing to answer him.

"Brother, submarines are very large ships, how can they float up and down, and be controlled by people's wishes?"

"Isn't there an air tank inside the submarine? The air tank is filled with a lot of air. If you want to make the submarine sink, then use a pump to push water into the air tank. You know that air has a kind of compressibility, turning a lot of air into an extremely small volume. Once the water enters, the air is compressed by the water. Thus, the weight of water is added to the submarine, so the submarine gradually sinks. If you want it to float up, then open the air tank opening to let the water flow out. At that time, the compressed air has a kind of expansion force, pushing the water out. The submarine becomes lighter, and then floats to the surface."

"I don't quite understand, brother, can you explain it again?"

"Don't understand? Okay, I'll tell you something very simple: you've seen crucian carp, right? It can float up from the bottom of the water, and then sink down from the surface of the water. Have you ever seen it? The principle of how it floats and sinks is the same as that of a submarine. It has a kind of swim bladder in its belly? This bladder is divided into a front chamber and a rear chamber. If it wants to float to the surface, then it spits out the water in the swim bladder, the air in the swim bladder expands, the fish's body becomes lighter, and it floats up. If it wants to sink, it eats more water into the swim bladder, the fish's body becomes heavier and it sinks."

"Brother, if it wants to float its head up and sink its tail down, then how does it do it?"

"If it wants to float its head up and sink its tail down, it just needs to add more water to the rear chamber of the swim bladder, and keep the front chamber free of water. Thus, the front chamber is lighter than the rear chamber, so the fish's head floats up and the fish's tail sinks down. Conversely, then the fish's tail will float up and the fish's tail will sink down."

Simple Darts, Bai Yi.

Little friends, I think you may have wanted to make a dart for a long time, right? Now let me tell you a method to make a simple dart: first take a slightly larger olive branch, and flatten the two pointed ends until there are several small holes at each end. (Small holes will definitely appear after grinding to a certain extent). Then take two or three long chicken feathers, and carefully insert them into the holes at one end; then take a steel needle and insert it into the holes at the other end, to the extent that it is stable and not easy to fall out. In this way, a pair of simple and fun little darts are made. You only need to throw it very lightly and it can be stably nailed to a wooden board or other loose materials.

Then, you can invite a few friends to compete to see who gets the most points by throwing darts at a target. You can also divide into two groups to compete, and you can also come up with new tricks to play. However, you have to be careful, don't aim at people like this: "shoot"!

Scientific Knowledge, The Reason Why You Can't Catch Your Breath, Zhang Yian.

Everyone knows the importance of air to people, right? Not eating for two or three days is not a big deal, but losing consciousness for ten minutes without breathing. Why? Because we need the oxygen in the air for nutrition every second. If the supply of oxygen stops, the blood in our bodies will stop flowing, the heart will lose its function, and life will be in danger.

When we move and walk, we need to use muscles. When muscles are used, they need more blood and oxygen for nutrition; the more vigorous the exercise, the more blood and oxygen nutrition is needed. Therefore, our breathing also becomes more rapid, and the heart also beats faster (because the heart is the central organ for transporting blood).

Sometimes, if the degree of vigorous exercise is too excessive, and the speed of your breathing cannot keep up with the nutrition needed by the muscles, you will have soreness and fatigue, and at the same time, you will not be able to catch your breath. If people with weak hearts force themselves to do strenuous exercise, then the heart's action will be too fast, to the extent that their hearts cannot handle it, and there is also a danger of losing their lives.

In sports fields or ball game fields, you often see some little friends trying to win the championship, forcing themselves to do exercises that they cannot handle, which is really worrying. The quality of sports performance depends entirely on consistent and effective daily practice. It cannot be achieved quickly in ten or eight days, and it cannot be won with one burst of effort. Even if you win, it will not only be useless to the body, but also harmful. Cautious schools must first ask a qualified doctor to examine the students' physical condition before determining whether they can learn a certain sport.

Don't Leave Your Schoolbag in School, Yushu.

Little friends often leave their schoolbags locked in the desks in the school in order to be convenient. This is a bad habit.

When we study, it is not enough to only attend classes in school for a few hours. All homework must be reviewed and studied at home. If you leave your schoolbag in school, and put all your books in your schoolbag, then what will you read at home at night? Even if you put a part of the books in your schoolbag, you must know that the school curriculum changes every day. You still have to take it when you need it the next day. Otherwise, you will definitely shout that you forgot to bring the book when class starts!

A schoolbag is not inconvenient to carry in your hand, and it is more troublesome to leave it in school. Little friends must have made this bad habit. You should reform it from today, and schools and families should try to correct it when they encounter this situation!

Electric Bell, Jing Tian.

Dear little friends! You have probably all seen electric bells; but do you know why when you press the protruding button in the small round wooden box (Figure 1) installed outside the door, the cone inside the leaf door rings?

Today I will discuss this issue with all of you little friends.

(The following picture is viewed horizontally, do not want the grid) Figure 1, Figure 2.

The electric bell is the simplest application of an electromagnet (Note 1). Its structure is shown in Figure 1.

In the figure, A is an electromagnet, B is the bell, C is a soft iron piece, D is a spring, attached to the soft iron piece, E is a hammer, one end connected to the soft iron piece, F is a nail, G, H are two metal pieces, I is a battery, and P is a button.

When I press the button outside the door, the two metal pieces touch each other, and the current passes through the electromagnet. The electromagnet then generates magnetism, thus attracting the soft iron piece in front. The hammer strikes the bell to make a sound once; at the same time, the contact point between the spring and the nail is separated, the current is interrupted, the electromagnet loses its magnetism, and the soft iron piece returns to its original position due to the spring force. The spring then contacts the nail again, the circuit is connected again, and the hammer strikes the bell again; because the time it takes for the spring to bounce back and the circuit to reconnect is extremely short, it is difficult for us to hear it. Therefore, if you do not release the button, the bell will continue to ring.

Note: Wind enameled wire, yarn-covered wire, etc., which are covered conductive wires, onto a pig iron rod in a spiral shape, and pass an electric current through the two ends. Then the pig iron rod becomes a magnet due to induction.

What Kind of Person Will I Be in the Future, Wang Dequan, Nanjing Municipal Xujiaxiang Elementary School. (Thirteenth Place)

Now the world powers, because their science is developed and production is surplus, not only do their own people use it, but they can also sell it abroad, absorbing the money of other countries. If a country with backward science, in this era of the survival of the fittest, absolutely has no independent existence.

Our country is an ancient country of East Asian civilization, and it is also a country that has been oppressed and invaded, and it is also a country with backward science. Some of the people are unwilling to humbly study science. All production relies on labor, so the output is very small, the value is very expensive, and the time is not economical. There are not enough goods for the people to use, so they have to buy from foreign countries. Therefore, large amounts of money flow out of the country, making the country poor and exhausted, with internal troubles and external disasters, and the people are miserable. Everything is oppressed, and the land is gradually lost, and the people often suffer disasters. It is all because of backward science. If this continues and is not remedied as soon as possible, not only will the lost land not be recovered, but even the country and nation may be difficult to preserve.

I hold a very grand and optimistic ambition, hoping to become a famous scientist in the future, in order to invent science and promote the progress of Chinese society. I believe that science and the country have a close relationship. Now only science can save China. Holding this determined ambition, in my study years, I will develop the habit of studying science, exploring scientific principles, hoping to make some inventions, and also teach my scientific thoughts to the people, so that the people of the whole country have scientific knowledge, creating a scientific country, restoring the people's happiness, revitalizing the country's industry, and recovering the country's lost land. In this way, the country will not perish, and the historical national humiliation will also be washed away cleanly.

The Tale of the Righteous Dog (16), Xin Qing.

(3)

That night, old Dashi lay on the bed frame in the corner of the wall and said, "Today is little Ailuo's naming day, isn't it?"

Little Nanluo made a gesture, answering his grandfather's question, he was very willing for the old man to forget about this matter and not mention it again. Old Dashi insisted on saying; "Why didn't you go to their house? Nanluo, you used to go every year."

Little Nanluo lowered his head and said softly on his grandfather's bed, "You are so sick, I can't leave you."

Old Dashi quickly said; "No need! No need! Grandma Follet will come to accompany me, it has happened many times before. Nanluo, why don't you go after all? Could it be that you had a quarrel with that outsider Doubei?"

Little Nanluo's face flushed red, and he quickly replied, "No, grandfather—nothing like that, it's really because Mr. Ke Ershi didn't invite me this year. He seems to be dissatisfied with me."

"But have you done anything wrong?"

"Not at all. I just drew a portrait of little Ailuo on a pine board."

"Alas!" Old Dashi sighed, and then remained silent, because the child's reply had made him understand everything. Although he was lying on the straw bed in the corner of the small house, he had not forgotten the ways of the world. He held little Nanluo's head in his arms, revealing a very loving expression.

He trembled slightly and said in a trembling voice, "My child, you are too poor! Too poor! How uncomfortable this makes you!"

Little Nanluo said softly: No, no, I am not poor, I am actually very rich. In fact, he secretly thought that he had the talent for painting, and his wealth far exceeded that of an emperor. At that moment, he walked to the door and stood in the quiet night, looking at the countless stars in the sky and the white poplars trembling in the wind.

All the rooms in the mill were brightly lit, and the sound of flutes was often blown over from the wind. Tears dripped from little Nanluo's face, but after a while, he put on a smiling face and said to himself, "Just wait for the future!" He lingered at the door for a long time, until the night was deep and everything was quiet, before returning to the house with Bradley and lying down to sleep together.

Little Nanluo had a secret that only Bradley knew. Next to the small house, there was another suite, which only he entered on weekdays. This was a very secluded place, but there was plenty of natural light shining in from the north. This was his studio. He used a rough piece of wood as a drawing board, and spread a large white sheet of paper for painting. All the impressions he had in his mind were drawn on it one by one.

No one had ever taught him about painting methods, and he didn't have any money to buy paints. Sometimes he couldn't even eat bread, so his paintings were never colored, but only black and white. He drew a very large portrait in lead powder; an old man sitting on a fallen tree, because he had seen the old woodcutter Laigel always sitting there at dusk.
