Shen Bao Local Supplement, Amateur Weekly Supplement News, The Preparation Process of the Sales Department of the Chinese Women's Production Cooperative, Ms. Fang Fan.

A few days ago, the writer saw the news in the newspaper that the Chinese Women's Production Cooperative was about to open, so she drove to visit Ms. Hu Ying, the manager of the cooperative, to inquire about the situation. She was told everything in detail. It is expected that this news will attract the attention of the community, so I discussed it with Ms. Hu and obtained her consent to publish her remarks as follows:

"Ms. Hu, you must be very busy now, right?"

"There is no particularly important work now. Please give me your instructions if you have anything to say."

"Your cooperative has been established for several years now, right? I really admire the efforts of you ladies for the society!"

"Don't dare! Don't dare! This is our due obligation, but we are not very good at running things, and we hope that people from all walks of life will give us more guidance. As for the past history of our cooperative, it is like this: because there are often many unemployed women who come to the Chinese Women's Temperance Association to ask for relief, Ms. Liu Wang Liming, the director of the association, feels the deepening of the current social depression. If there is no more practical way, there is no way to provide relief. So, in the spring of last year, she initiated the organization of the Chinese Women's Production Cooperative, leading them to use their own abilities to help themselves. In the past year, the results have been pretty good. Now we feel that this organization should be expanded and popularized, so we passed it through the board of directors and appointed several comrades to prepare for it in a hurry."

"Then what are the purposes and business nature and scope of your cooperative?"

"We feel that the crux of gender inequality mainly lies in the weak economic capacity of women. Many female compatriots are not necessarily incompetent, but because they have very few outlets in any aspect. At the same time, the products they produce cannot be sold far and wide for various reasons, just like the market of capitalist monopoly colonies. All markets are monopolized by men, so women have to bury their inherent abilities and become profit-sharers or victims of men. Now, the purpose of our cooperative, in addition to the calligraphy and painting department to promote women's culture and art, is to help the general laboring female compatriots sell their products, so that they can be sold well in the market and no longer be exploited by the middle class, so as to improve women's production and promote their economic independence. As for the business scope, it is temporarily divided into three departments.

The calligraphy and painting department only sells the products of Chinese female painters and female writers. However, the scope of books is wider, because many books on women and family issues should also be collected to meet the needs of readers.

The food department has an inseparable relationship between diet and hygiene, and the preparation of food is also a skill of women, so it is listed as a department.

Crafts have always been very historical in China. Since the eastward spread of European styles, people have valued machine-made products and inevitably ignored handicrafts. But science is indeed omnipotent, and manual labor also has its inherent advantages, so our cooperative also regards it as a basic part. For the time being, it is limited to the above three departments, but it can be expanded at any time. As long as it is a product of women, it can be sold by our cooperative, but this is purely a cooperative nature, and only a very small part of the proceeds from the sale is taken as a handling fee for our cooperative." Ms. Hu Ying, Manager and Director of Calligraphy and Painting Department of the Cooperative.

"Can you tell me about the preparation process and future policy of your cooperative?"

"Yes, since the board of directors resolved to add a sales department, it immediately approved a new Western-style store at No. 205 Yuanmingyuan Road, which is currently being renovated, and appointed the responsible personnel to start carrying out everything. Because we are divided into three departments here, each department must have a director to plan everything. Now that we are just starting out, things are still simple, so the position of director of the calligraphy and painting department is temporarily held by me. For all products of the department, the "painting" industry has already obtained the consent of several ladies from the Chinese Women's Calligraphy and Painting Association, Feng Wenfeng, Chen Xiaocui, Yang Xuejiu, Li Qiujun, Wu Qingxia, Yu Jingzhi, Gu Qingyao, Zhou Lianxia, Xu Lengcui, and Jin Qiusheng, who have agreed to supply their best works to our cooperative: "Books" have also been discussed with major bookstores such as Women's Bookstore, Beixin Bookstore, Zhonghua Bookstore, Commercial Press, and Life Bookstore to supply works by famous female writers such as Bing Xin, Ding Ling, Lu Yin, Xie Bingying, Yu Qingtang, and Shen Ziju to our cooperative. Ms. Liu Wang Liming, the founder of the cooperative.

Page 20

And works on women and family issues will be supplied to our cooperative, and Ms. Liu Wang Liming's own literary creation "The Waves of Life" will also be published; the meticulous constructions of the above ladies have long been popular at home and abroad, and there is no need for me to introduce them. The director of the crafts department is Ms. Zhang Xuehai. The items in this department include embroidery, manufacturing, and other handmade products. In addition to the Women's Home Affairs Advanced Vocational School and the Women and Children Education Institute taking charge of a part, the rest have been contacted in various aspects such as Beiping Shaoxing. The director of the food department is Ms. Wu Shuqing. The focus of the products in this department is on Chinese and Western refreshments, which are completely the results of the Home Affairs School. There are also several other staff members who assist together. However, we all take serving the society as our duty, so there is no salary. Unless the cooperative has a surplus, after deducting expenses and running charitable undertakings, everyone can share it equally. However, we still need to hire a female staff member who can speak fluent English and has some knowledge of bookkeeping. If there is such a talent and is interested in serving the society, they can describe their strengths in detail and write a letter to me—No. 14 Yuanchangli, Hualong Road—to contact me. As for the future policy, there is really nothing I can tell you, but at present, our women are always more or less under double or even triple oppression, which is undeniable. All undertakings related to women are still in the budding stage. There are certainly many supporters, but there will definitely be no shortage of people who intend to destroy them. I sincerely hope that everyone can work together to promote it slowly from Shanghai to the whole country. We know that in the current era of economic panic, it is not easy to run any undertaking well, but if you cannot fight against the bad environment and overcome all difficulties, then you will have no way out."

"Ms. Hu, you have extensive contacts, and you are certainly competent for the position of manager. Would you be willing to announce some of your resume and private life?"

"I am really ashamed to have been entrusted with this important task this time. Although the Chinese and Western directors of the Women's Temperance Association decided to appoint me, I always feel that I have spent too long in school life, and I am really still a student rather than a businessman. Although I have served in the political world for more than a year since leaving Peking University, and then ran around in the education and business circles for seven or eight years, according to my past experience, if I make a self-criticism, I am afraid I will not be able to be competent. Fortunately, I have the encouragement and support of friends from all walks of life, and the help of so many comrades. Just taking the competence and competence of the two ladies Zhang and Wu here is enough to be my good helpers, so I will reluctantly do my best, otherwise it may be inevitable to exceed the limit. As for my private life, it is really too simple. Except for reading a little Japanese at the Liangcai Supplementary School every night, there is nothing I can report. And the Women's Monthly Magazine has sent someone to interview me the day before yesterday, so to avoid repetition, I won't say more. Speaking of extensive contacts, I really dare not say that. It has only been ten years since I stepped into society. The people I know in the military, police, political, business, and academic circles are only a few thousand people. As for those who are relatively high-status in society, there are only a few hundred people. How can that be enough to be called contacts?"

"I heard that Ms. Hu is also a member of the Chinese Women's Calligraphy and Painting Association founded by Ms. Tang Guanyu. When your cooperative opens in the future, there will probably be a lot of your works, right?"

"It's very embarrassing. Although there is one work with the inscription Hu Xin, it is my humble work, but I have never had time to practice. It is just a kind of pastime in my spare time. I remember that three years ago, I was commissioned by Mr. Xie Wuliang, Chen Liting, Xu Beihong, Zhang Shizhao and other gentlemen to set a remuneration example for me, but I am afraid that there are still less than a hundred large and small calligraphy pieces that I have responded to from all walks of life. I am really unfamiliar. I hope that all major experts will give me more advice in the future."

Current Affairs Research, The Discordant Anglo-French Relationship, Zhao Qi.

Both Britain and France are major supporters of the League of Nations. Diplomats in London and Paris have always used Geneva to their advantage. In this respect, it can be said that they have no conflict. But the main goal of British diplomacy after the war was to strive to maintain the balance of power in Europe, in order to preserve the British Empire's inherent position in Europe, and to maintain its rights in African and Asian colonies; while France's diplomatic vision was focused on the other side of the Rhine River, focused on Berlin; therefore, although the diplomatic policies of Britain and France were both based on the League of Nations, their respective goals were fundamentally different, which made it difficult for London and Paris to combine their wills fundamentally.

Recently, because Mussolini's expedition to Africa attempted to monopolize Abyssinia, the British felt that their African colonies were threatened, and the original power on the Mediterranean Sea was shaken. Therefore, when the news of the Italian-Ethiopian war broke out, Britain immediately shouted loudly in Geneva, implementing sanctions against Italy. Since France is also a supporter of the League of Nations, it is certainly inconvenient to openly leave Geneva and clearly support Italy's aggression; but in order to defend Germany, France and Italy had signed the Rome Agreement. In the hearts of Parisian diplomats, they naturally did not want to abandon their new friend, and follow the British to deal with Italy; therefore, in contradiction, France adopted a conciliatory and all-encompassing attitude towards the Italian-Ethiopian issue. On the one hand, it continued to negotiate with Britain in Geneva, superficially respecting the League of Nations Covenant, and on the other hand, it secretly courted Rome, expressing its unwillingness to actively implement sanctions. As a result, British imperialism was certainly greatly unhappy, but other than being unhappy, there was no active way to deal with it for a while; and because there were no other good friends, they had to pretend to smile and continue to talk with Paris, dreaming that the Anglo-French relationship could be reconciled under a united front against Italy.

At the same time, just when the British-Italian conflict was acute and Britain and France could not agree, like a bolt from the blue, on the 7th of last month, Hitler suddenly declared the abolition of the Treaty of Locarno, marched into the Rhineland, and put forward six points of opinions as the basis for international peace negotiations. His excuse was that France's signing of a mutual assistance pact with the Soviet Union had violated the spirit of the Treaty of Locarno, so this treaty did not need to be observed, and the German army's entry into the Rhineland was justified. This was simply a blatant act of aggression and challenge to France. Therefore, France's response to Hitler's act of destroying the treaty, in addition to mobilizing troops and deploying them to the border, was to run to Geneva to shout about the crisis on the banks of the Rhine, and to demand that the signatory countries of the Treaty of Locarno and the League of Nations sanction Germany. But at this time, the Italian army invading Ethiopia had advanced to the Lake Tana region, and Britain was watching its rights on the Nile River with open eyes. The response to France's request was to pay more attention to the East African war, saying that European security could not be maintained until the East African problem was resolved. When the French peace plan was put forward, Berlin considered it to be "a towering skyscraper," Geneva considered it to be "a fanciful and ambitious plan that could not be implemented," and London's attitude was also very cold. On the 18th of this month, British Prime Minister Baldwin gave a speech in Hawasett, in addition to fiercely attacking Italy, he openly said that Hitler had "the greatest power to dispel the gloom in all of Europe." This situation was of course very displeasing to France. But in order to deal with Germany, and in order not to allow the British to openly support Hitler's treaty-breaking behavior, it still had to continue negotiations with London, requesting British military assistance. Although the British, French and even Belgian diplomats and staff have not discussed an effective solution for the continuous negotiations on the Rhineland issue, diplomatic negotiations still have to be carried out, because although they have their own agendas, although they cannot come together in the current situation, they are not willing to break up right away.

Because of the discordant Anglo-French relationship, Mussolini and Hitler, these two ambitious people, can of course run more boldly on their dangerous paths. In fact, because France is easing the sanction atmosphere in Geneva, the Italian army invading Ethiopia not only does not stop attacking, but also uses poison gas unscrupulously to poison unarmed Ethiopian people. Now the Italian army has occupied Taixi and is approaching the Ethiopian capital. The British rights on the Nile River have felt a more realistic threat, and the British-Italian conflict has developed into a more direct situation, but this, in addition to making the nerves of the British Empire tense, Paris is still maintaining its leisurely attitude towards this situation. On the other hand, after Hitler created the fact that the German army entered the Rhineland, he worked hard to build defense projects there, and expressed his intention to recover the lost colonies; at the same time, he also put forward many new suggestions and new problems in order to win over London's desires and attempt to shift Western Europe's attention to Eastern Europe. This kind of performance will certainly not shift Britain's gaze from the Nile River, but it is an intolerable attack for Paris. Therefore, under the British toleration of Hitler's treaty-breaking behavior, France has even recently expressed its intention to act freely and independently. At present, Geneva is paying close attention to the Nile and Rhine issues, but this attention comes from London and Paris. Therefore, there are two voices of sanctions in Geneva at present: one is to intensify sanctions against Italy as soon as possible, and the other is to implement sanctions against Germany. It goes without saying that the former is advocated by Britain, but France is easing the situation from it; conversely, the latter is advocated by France, but Britain is advising Parisian politicians not to "act emotionally."

According to a report on the 21st of this month, as a result of the Eden-Pengu talks, Britain and France have made concessions to each other and reached a compromise. In this compromise, what Eden got was: "France must not act emotionally and withdraw from the League of Nations in a fit of anger, because although the League of Nations has no power to solve the Rhineland issue, if France breaks away from the League of Nations, the Nile issue will become more difficult. France must not cancel the current sanctions against Italy, and must continue to abide by the League of Nations Covenant. Regarding the Rhineland issue, Britain should negotiate with Germany, so that the peace plans proposed by Germany and France can be considered at the same time; but for national affairs, time must be given so that Britain can proceed calmly. "As for what Pengu got was: "Although the current sanctions against Italy can be maintained, they do not need to be intensified. Britain must treat the Rhineland incident and the Italian-Ethiopian dispute equally, and must not be biased, so as to avoid increasing Germany's arrogance, resulting in another act of destroying the treaty, and Italy will not be quickly disappointed, so that the country has prepared to rejoin the European collective security organization. Regarding the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, the British and French governments must cooperate sincerely to find a peaceful solution. "Such a so-called compromise, although on the surface shows the mutual concern between Britain and France, the so-called "friendly spirit," but in reality, France did not abandon Italy and actively help Britain; similarly, Britain did not abandon its attitude of tolerating Hitler and stood on the side of France and resolutely implemented the obligations of international treaties. In fact, on the first day after this so-called compromise was reached, the opinions of the British and French representatives at the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations were also significantly inconsistent, which exposed the "crack" in the structure of the League of Nations. According to Eden's speech, Italy violated the League of Nations Covenant and should be dealt with in a consistent manner; but Pengu said that to deal with the threats in Europe, Italy must cooperate fully. - This expression has fully explained that the so-called Anglo-French compromise is only to a certain extent, and it is superficial; the spirit of London and Paris has not yet reached a consensus.

However, under such a discordant Anglo-French relationship, first, Germany and Italy will inevitably become bolder and move towards a dangerous path, thus causing the conflict between Britain and Italy and between France and Germany to become more acute. Now, the Italian army has occupied the Guberra area bordering British and Egyptian Sudan, facing the British army and air force stationed there from afar, so the armed conflict between Britain and Italy is on the verge of breaking out. As for the relationship between Germany and France, although there is not necessarily a very possible outbreak of war, under the British tolerance and encouragement, Hitler's constant adventurous actions may ignite the European fire line at any time. Secondly, due to the inability of Britain and France to agree, the League of Nations will become a useless organization that cannot solve problems, and the situation in Europe and even the world will become more chaotic.

At the same time, following Germany's announcement of the abolition of the Treaty of Locarno, there is also Hungary's rearmament and expansion, and Turkey's restoration of military equipment in the straits. These are all sufficient to make the European situation more tense and chaotic.

International Commercial Telegram - Special Commercial Report from Reuters, April 25th 79

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today, the price eased slightly, dropping half a penny from yesterday, to 140 shillings and 11 pence.

London Raw Silver: Today's market was slightly sluggish. Spot and futures prices were both 20 pence 375, each dropping .625. China sold, and India made slight purchases.

Mount Lyell Copper: This morning, the opening market eased due to long positions being closed. The July contract fell 45 pounds, settling at 45.24-46.60.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was slightly mixed this morning. The price of the pound was firm. The opening British-American exchange rate was $4.935625, slightly down .03125 from yesterday's American-British closing rate, but it rose .125 after one hour, to $4.936875, and continued rising .125 at closing, reaching $4.938125.

Securities

New York: The stock market opened slightly weaker this morning due to speculative closing of positions, but security prices rose internally. Steel and copper stocks rose more sharply. After a few minutes, the market turned quiet and fluctuated. Steel, copper, and rail stocks all fell due to selling pressure. Demand for oil stocks was still good. At 11 o'clock, shares of Delaware, Lackawanna and Western Railroad common stock fell, but the price was still higher than yesterday's closing. Oil stocks were firm. Shares of New Jersey Standard Oil were strong, up one pound from yesterday's close due to speculative buying. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left.

Cotton and Wheat: The New York cotton market opened today at 1.28 due to purchases of both near- and far-term contracts by dealers and speculators. At 11 o'clock, the market price fell again due to the closing of long positions. The July contract fell to 11.24, down one pound from yesterday's closing. The drought in the wheat region has not yet subsided.

Liverpool Cotton Market: Today, American cotton futures were stable. The May contract closed at 6.26, the same as yesterday's close.

Chicago Wheat: This morning, futures opened weaker due to the closing of long positions. The July contract fell .875, to 90.875, but favorable weather reports for the long position maintained the market and triggered speculative buying. Shortly after the opening, the July contract recovered .375, but at 11 o'clock, the market turned weaker again. The July contract fell another .125, to 91.125, a net decrease of .625 from yesterday's closing. The feed grain market was weak, and prices tended to move in line with wheat prices.

Liverpool Wheat: Today was firm. The May contract closed at 6 shillings and 2.5 pence, half a penny higher than yesterday.

Rubber

(London) Today's rubber prices, the July and September contracts closed at 7 pence 625, the same as yesterday's closing.

New York: The rubber market opened slightly stronger this morning due to purchases by dealers. The July contract rose two pounds sterling, to 16.07. Later, the market was sluggish and uneventful. The July contract returned to the opening price. The New York commodity market prices are listed on the left.

U.S. Naval Exercises: 150 Warships, 400 Aircraft to Practice Defense of Hawaiian Islands 80

San Diego, California: The U.S. Fleet began Exercise No. 17 today. Six submarine tenders have already sailed to the Panama Canal. On Monday, more destroyers, aircraft carriers, and battleships will sail south from here and San Pedro Harbor. The exercise will last six weeks. The fleet participating includes 150 warships, 400 aircraft, and 45,000 soldiers, under the command of Rear Admiral Reeves, the Commander of the Fleet. This is Reeves' last chance to demonstrate his abilities, as he will be promoted to the Naval General Staff on June 1 and retire on December 1. The nature of this exercise is currently kept secret, but it is said to be a continuation of last year's Exercise No. 16 and related to the defense of Hawaii. (24th National Telegram)

(Washington) The House Naval Committee submitted a report today requesting the passage of an appropriation of $175,000,000 for auxiliary vessels. The report also stated that the Pacific coast extends for more than 2,000 miles, and there are very few shipyards for repairing warships. If a war breaks out with a major power in the Pacific, the defense of the West Coast will be seriously affected. Therefore, it is necessary to take remedial measures as soon as possible. (24th National Telegram)

A Glimpse of Italian Construction: Swamps Can Become Plains, New City to Be Built, Groundbreaking Ceremony Held Yesterday 81

(Rome) The Pontine Marshes, originally a swamp, have been transformed into a plain after recent construction and filling. The government plans to build a new city on the site, named the City of Aprilia. The groundbreaking ceremony was held recently. Villagers from nearby areas arrived in droves, creating a very enthusiastic atmosphere. Prime Minister Mussolini personally attended and presided over the ceremony, giving a speech saying, "It has been 160 days since the League of Nations imposed economic sanctions on Italy. During this long period, the chaos and poverty of the world have increased, but our country's indomitable will and calm response have been clearly demonstrated. After the City of Aprilia's groundbreaking today, it will be officially completed on October 29, 1937. In addition, we plan to build the City of Pomezia, which will be completed on October 29, 1939. By then, our work will be completed, and another new victory will be added to the glorious history of Italy." After the Prime Minister finished his speech, he personally held a hoe, drawing a line on the ground as the boundary of the new city, and then left in a car amidst the cheers of the villagers. (25th Havas Dispatch)

British League of Nations Association Calls for Stepped-Up Sanctions and Closure of Suez Canal 82

(London) The Confederation of League of Nations Unions has recently resolved to demand that the government step up sanctions against Italy and close the Suez Canal so that peace in East Africa can be quickly restored. (24th Havas Dispatch)

(London) The Confederation of League of Nations Unions met in Edinburgh last night. Lord Lytton (former Chairman of the League of Nations Manchuria Inquiry Commission) delivered a speech, stating, "The international situation has reached a desperate point and should be dealt with by burning one's boats in order to achieve success. Italy has expressed its determination to complete the invasion of Abyssinia, and the sanctions decided by the League of Nations have not been able to stop it. Therefore, the only way to stop the East African war is to close the Suez Canal to cut off Italy's communication with East Africa. Foreign Secretary Eden will submit a proposal for closure when the League of Nations Council meets next month on the 11th, and he has stated that if the Council decides to proceed, Britain will comply." (25th Havas Dispatch)

(London) Political figures recently declared that the Confederation of League of Nations Unions is now actively promoting the League of Nations, and Lord Lytton's speech in Edinburgh last night can be seen as a 'desperate plea' from the sanction advocates to the Cabinet, and the impact may even lead to the dissolution of the Cabinet. Well-informed sources believe that Foreign Secretary Eden may agree to the proposal for stepped-up sanctions, but Prime Minister Baldwin opposed it. The Confederation of League of Nations Unions held a plebiscite last spring to gauge public support for the League of Nations' principles. The results showed that out of 12 million votes, 9,627,606 voted in favor of unconditional economic sanctions, and 6,506,777 voted in favor of taking military sanctions (if necessary) to stop acts of aggression. It can be seen from this that the Confederation has the support of national public opinion. (25th Havas Dispatch)
